# Changelog

All notable changes to Mr. Bridge are documented here.
Format: [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.1.0/)

---

## [Unreleased]

### Fixed
- **WCAG 2.1 AA color-contrast вҖ” axe sweep re-enabled (#381).**
  - Added `--accent-text: oklch(45% 0.13 65)` in light mode (вүҲ5:1 on page bg) alongside existing `--accent`; dark mode aliases `--accent-text` to `--accent` unchanged.
  - Darkened light-mode `--color-text-on-cta` from near-white `oklch(98% 0 0)` to dark ink `oklch(16% 0.020 var(--hue))` вҖ” fixes near-white-on-amber pill fills (notifications filter, settings theme radio, window-selector pills).
  - Updated all Pattern A consumers (amber-as-text) to use `--accent-text`: nav active links/icons, journal outer/inner tabs, meals settings links, macro summary settings link, meals "Add macros"/"Ingredients"/"Estimate macros" action links, meals chat link.
  - Removed `data-reveal` from the desktop nav (`position: fixed`) вҖ” the entrance animation started at `opacity: 0`, causing axe to evaluate link text at reduced opacity and produce spurious timing-dependent failures.
  - Re-enabled `color-contrast` rule in `smoke/specs/a11y.spec.ts` (removed `.disableRules(["color-contrast"])` + TODO comment). All 11 routes now pass the axe critical/serious gate.

### Added
- **Calendar tab вҖ” week/day/month views with full CRUD (#375).**
  - New `/calendar` route with a full-height calendar surface. Week view is the default; toggle to Day or Month via the view pill in the toolbar. Prev/next navigation and "Today" jump button.
  - Week/day view: 24-hour scrollable time grid (starts at 7 AM), events positioned absolutely by start/end time, greedy overlap detection shows simultaneous events side-by-side. All-day events rendered in a banner row above the grid. Current-time indicator line.
  - Month view: 7-column grid with event pills (up to 3 per day, "+N more" overflow label).
  - Click any empty slot вҶ’ create-event modal (title, date, start/end time, all-day toggle, location). Click any event вҶ’ detail dialog (time, location, calendar label) with Edit and Delete (two-tap confirm) actions.
  - `calendarType` (primary / birthday / holiday / other) maps to distinct accent colors across all views.
  - New API routes: `GET /api/google/calendar/range?timeMin=&timeMax=` for range queries; `POST /api/google/calendar/events` to create; `PATCH /api/google/calendar/events/[eventId]` to update; `DELETE /api/google/calendar/events/[eventId]` to delete.
  - Demo mode: `DEMO_CALENDAR_EVENTS` extended from 4 to 20 events spanning 3 weeks (all-day, birthday, holiday, overlapping, and multi-hour events) so all three views are populated with meaningful data.
  - Calendar nav item (CalendarDays icon) added between Weekly and Journal; appears in the "More" bottom sheet on mobile.
  - All colors use existing CSS tokens (`--accent`, `--accent-soft`, `--rule-soft`, etc.); no raw hex in `.tsx` files вҖ” token-lint clean.


- **Per-user Oura and Fitbit token storage in `user_integrations` (#394, #395).** Oura and Fitbit are now multi-tenant:
  - **Oura:** Users paste a Personal Access Token in Settings вҶ’ Integrations (inline expand). Token is stored encrypted in `user_integrations` (provider `"oura"`). `syncOura` reads from the table first, falls back to `OURA_ACCESS_TOKEN` env var (owner migration path). Python `scripts/sync-oura.py` updated to use `_integrations.py` helper with the same priority.
  - **Fitbit:** New `/api/auth/fitbit/start` + `/api/auth/fitbit/callback` OAuth 2.0 routes (mirrors Google pattern: CSRF cookie, Basic auth code exchange, `storeIntegration`). `syncFitbit` reads refresh token from `user_integrations` first, falls back to `profile` table. Token rotation writes back to the same source via `persistRotatedToken`. Python `scripts/sync-fitbit.py` updated similarly.
  - **UI:** Integrations settings panel now shows Oura and Fitbit rows (connected badge + Disconnect server action when connected; Connect Oura inline paste field / Connect Fitbit OAuth button when not).
  - **New env var:** `FITBIT_OAUTH_REDIRECT_URI` вҖ” required for Fitbit OAuth (app-level, not per-user). `FITBIT_CLIENT_ID` / `FITBIT_CLIENT_SECRET` unchanged.
  - **New helper:** `scripts/_integrations.py` mirrors `web/src/lib/integrations/tokens.ts` for Python scripts, using the same Supabase encrypt/decrypt RPCs.

- **Expandable exercise description/tips panel and in-app rest timer (#414, #283).**
  - `description` (string) and `tips` (string[]) optional fields added to `WorkoutExercise` in types and the `assign_workout` / `update_workout_exercise` tool schemas. The AI now populates 1вҖ“3 sentence how-to descriptions and 2вҖ“4 form cues per exercise at plan generation time.
  - Each `ExerciseRow` in the weekly workout plan shows a `в–ҫ` chevron button when `description` or `tips` data is present. Tapping it collapses/expands an inline panel with the description paragraph and a tips bullet list. Exercises without these fields are unaffected.
  - `InlineSetLogger` now starts a rest countdown automatically after each successful set log. Duration defaults to 90 s; override via `localStorage` key `bridge:rest_timer_duration`. The timer persists across page reloads via `bridge:rest_timer_end`. Dismissible with вң•. On completion a gentle pulse animation plays and an optional ntfy.sh push fires via a new `/api/notifications/push` route (requires `NTFY_TOPIC` env var; silent if unset).
  - New Settings вҶ’ Fitness section with a rest-timer On/Off toggle backed by the profile kv key `rest_timer_enabled`.

- **Workout improvements: weight notation, fitness tabs, personal records (#331).**
  - `weight_notation` field (`per_hand` | `total` | `null`) on `WorkoutExercise` вҖ” Bridge now writes it for new exercises; existing dumbbell exercises auto-infer `per_hand` at render time via name pattern match. Weight display shows "/ hand" or "total" muted label next to target weights throughout the plan and logged sets.
  - `/fitness` page refactored into a tabbed surface (Dashboard / Workouts / History) using a new `FitnessClient` client component. Dashboard (body comp, recovery, activity trends) is the default landing tab.
  - `exercise_prs` Supabase table stores pre-computed PRs (weight, rep, volume) per exercise per user. PRs are upserted after each session completion; first-load backfill runs once if the table is empty. рҹҸҶ chip appears inline on exercises with a PR set in the last 30 days. Full PR table (weight PR, rep PR, volume, date) lives under History.
- **Equipment inventory + cancel/reschedule-workout support (#370).** Three new capabilities:
  - New `user_equipment` table (RLS-enabled) with composite unique `NULLS NOT DISTINCT` on `(user_id, equipment_type, weight_lbs, resistance_level)`. New Settings вҶ’ Equipment section where you can add/remove equipment by type, weight, resistance level, and quantity. Stock types: dumbbell pair, barbell, plate set, kettlebell, resistance band, slider.
  - New `get_user_equipment` Bridge tool returns a structured `{ items, maxes }` map. `assign_workout` and `update_workout_exercise` now validate proposed weights against inventory before writing вҖ” reject with a truth-in-payload error listing each violation and the available max (per #346). System prompt updated: Bridge always calls `get_user_equipment` before proposing weights and never exceeds inventory limits.
  - Workout plan status column (`planned | completed | cancelled | skipped`, default `planned`) with `cancel_reason` and `cancelled_at`. Backfill migration marks plans with linked `strength_sessions` as `completed`, all others remain `planned`. New `cancel_workout` Bridge tool soft-cancels the DB row and deletes the Google Calendar event in one atomic operation with read-after-write verification on both (per #319). Cancel action added to the Fitness tab weekly plan вҖ” "Cancel workout" button in each expanded plan row (planned status only); confirmed cancelled rows render dimmed with strikethrough and a "Cancelled" badge.
  - New `reschedule_workout` Bridge tool moves a planned workout atomically: copies config to target date, soft-cancels source, PATCHes (not recreates) the existing calendar event to the new date preserving event ID and attendees. New shared logic in `web/src/lib/fitness/` consumed by both tools and the server action.

### Changed
- **Cron now syncs Oura, Fitbit, and Google Fit for all connected users, not just the owner (#420).** `web/src/app/api/cron/sync/route.ts` replaces the single-owner `syncOura/syncFitbit/syncGoogleFit(db, ownerUserId)` calls with a per-provider fan-out:
  - `listConnectedUsers(db, provider)` (already in `web/src/lib/integrations/tokens.ts:86`, zero callers before this PR) fetches all `user_id` values for a given provider from `user_integrations`.
  - `Promise.allSettled` runs each user's sync concurrently; one user's failure does not abort others.
  - Response shape changes from `{ updated: N }` to `{ usersSynced: N, usersFailed: N, errors: [{userId, error}] }` per provider.
  - The 30-min skip window remains a **global gate per provider** (`lastSyncAgeSecs` is not user-scoped; no schema change to `sync_log`).
  - Stocks and sports syncs remain owner-scoped (`OWNER_USER_ID` still required); `OWNER_USER_ID` env var is unchanged.

- **Meal API routes migrated to ToolLoopAgent.generate() (#366).** All four `generateText()` call sites under `web/src/app/api/meals/` now use `new ToolLoopAgent({ model, instructions, output }).generate({ messages })` вҖ” the same config surface as the chat agent. `suggest/route.ts` and both modes in `analyze-photo/route.ts` use `claude-sonnet-4-6`; `estimate-macros/route.ts` retains `claude-haiku-4-5-20251001`. Instructions are extracted from the embedded prompt text into the `instructions` constructor param; user-facing dynamic content remains in the `messages` payload. No behaviour or response shape changes. Prompt caching follow-up tracked in #340.

### Fixed
- **Chat smoke no longer fails when Google isn't connected on the smoke account (#420).** `web/smoke/specs/chat.spec.ts` clears the `consoleErrors` array immediately after `page.goto("/chat")`. Root cause: login redirects to `/dashboard`, which mounts `ScheduleToday`, `UpcomingBirthday`, and `ImportantEmails` вҖ” all three fire client-side fetches to `/api/google/calendar`, `/api/google/calendar/upcoming-birthday`, and `/api/google/gmail`, which return 403 when the smoke user has no Google tokens. The fixture accumulates errors across the full page session, so those pre-navigation 403s were counted against the chat test's `consoleErrors.toHaveLength(0)` assertion.

- **CI smoke workflow now has Google OAuth creds (#417).** Added `GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID` and `GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET` to both the `smoke-pr` and `smoke-release` env blocks in [.github/workflows/smoke.yml](.github/workflows/smoke.yml). Without them, Next dev-server boot hit `throw new Error("Missing GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID or GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET env vars")` in [web/src/lib/google-auth.ts](web/src/lib/google-auth.ts) on the first chat-tool module import, failing every PR's smoke run. Required repo secrets: `GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID`, `GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET` (add via Settings вҶ’ Secrets and variables вҶ’ Actions; same values as Vercel prod).

- **Push notifications restored and tap-to-open fixed (#383).** Root causes: (1) `APP_URL` was missing from `.env` вҖ” every check script calls `os.environ.get("APP_URL", "")` and silently skips the `--click-url` argument when it's empty, so all ntfy.sh Click headers were dropped. Added `APP_URL=https://mr-bridge-assistant.vercel.app` to `.env`. (2) No cron entries existed вҖ” the five check scripts were never scheduled. `scripts/install-notifications.sh` now writes idempotent cron entries for all five scripts with correct schedules (weather 07:00, daily-alerts 07:30, birthdays 08:00, HRV 08:30, tasks 09:00 + 17:00). Each cron entry sources `.env` before invoking the script so env vars are available outside a shell session. (3) `notify.sh` had no delivery log вҖ” silent curl failures were invisible. Now appends one ISO-timestamped line per attempt to `~/.mr-bridge/notify.log` whether or not `NTFY_TOPIC` is set.

- **Bridge no longer stalls mid-turn after announcing a next action (#369).** Added a system-prompt rule requiring Bridge to either call the corresponding tool in the same turn or end with an explicit confirmation question when it writes a promissory statement ("Now assigning X", "Next I'll...", "Moving on to..."). Root cause was the per-step confirmation cadence (calendar pre-flight, delete/update guards) being over-generalised to every tool call in a bulk-approved batch. Prompt-only fix; no agent-loop or TypeScript changes.
- **Past-day habit cells now persist on click (#386).** `toggleHabit` was using `onConflict: "habit_id,date"` which no longer matched the actual unique constraint `(user_id, habit_id, date)` introduced in migration `20260417000001` вҖ” upserts on existing rows silently did nothing. Fixed the conflict target to `"user_id,habit_id,date"`. Also added error checking on both the upsert and delete paths (`{ error }` was previously discarded), so failures now throw and the client's existing optimistic-rollback in `handleCellClick` correctly fires. Delete filter extended with `.eq("user_id", user.id)` to match the upsert scope.

### Changed
- **Email multi-account ingestion migrated off Gmail POP3 to auto-forwarding (#391).** Google is deprecating the "Check mail from other accounts (POP)" feature in 2026 вҖ” new users lost access in Q1 2026, existing users lose access before year-end. No Mr. Bridge code changes required: the `Professional` label detection in `/api/google/gmail` and the dashboard `important-emails` widget are transport-agnostic (they key off the label, not the delivery mechanism). Updated `docs/gmail-multi-account.md` with auto-forwarding setup instructions (enable forward on secondary вҶ’ verify address вҶ’ Gmail filter on primary to apply `Professional` label вҶ’ decommission old POP source). Updated `.claude/rules/briefing.md` and `README.md` to remove POP3 references.

### Added
- **Impeccable UI revamp complete (#272).** Phase A (universal design system + dashboard) and Phase B (all 11 surfaces + nav shell) shipped. Gate B verification passed вҖ” all automated checks clean (CLS=0, LCP <1200ms desktop / <2100ms mobile, zero inline padding/duration literals, Phase A dead files removed). Follow-ups: #381 (color contrast), #384 (mobile LCP/CLS).
- **Per-user Google OAuth refresh tokens вҖ” multi-tenant Google integrations (#390).** Replaces the single global `GOOGLE_REFRESH_TOKEN` env var with per-user rows in a new `user_integrations` Supabase table. Each user connects their own Google account via `/settings вҶ’ Integrations` ("Connect Google" button вҶ’ Google consent screen вҶ’ callback stores the encrypted refresh token). New `encrypt_integration_token` / `decrypt_integration_token` SQL functions wrap `pgp_sym_encrypt` / `pgp_sym_decrypt` keyed by a new `ENCRYPTION_KEY` env var вҖ” first use of column-level encryption in this codebase. `getGoogleAuthClient` is now async and per-user; falls back to the `GOOGLE_REFRESH_TOKEN` env var for the owner until the seed script is run post-deploy (zero-downtime migration). All 12 `getGoogleAuthClient` call sites updated: chat tools (`calendar.ts` 4 sites, `gmail.ts` 2, `workouts.ts` 2) and API routes (`/api/google/calendar`, `/api/google/calendar/upcoming-birthday`, `/api/google/gmail`). Google Fit sync helper (`getGoogleAccessToken`) similarly migrated вҖ” drops `GOOGLE_FIT_REFRESH_TOKEN` and `GOOGLE_FIT_CLIENT_ID/SECRET` env vars. OAuth start route at `/api/auth/google/start` and callback at `/api/auth/google/callback` (greenfield вҖ” no prior auth-code flow existed). Disconnect deletes the row via a settings server action. API routes now return `{ not_connected: true, status: 403 }` instead of a generic 500 when `GoogleNotConnectedError` is thrown. One-shot seed script at `scripts/seed-owner-google-integration.ts` moves the owner's existing token into the DB post-deploy. **Post-deploy manual steps:** (1) add `ENCRYPTION_KEY` to Vercel env; (2) add redirect URIs to Google Cloud Console OAuth client; (3) run `npx tsx scripts/seed-owner-google-integration.ts`. Closes #390, unblocks #380.

### Removed
- **`OURA_ACCESS_TOKEN` and `FITBIT_REFRESH_TOKEN` env-var / profile-table fallbacks removed (#421).** PR #419 moved tokens into `user_integrations`; PR #420 confirmed cron reads from there for all users; owner has since connected both providers via Settings вҶ’ Integrations. `syncOura` now throws immediately if `loadIntegration` returns null (no `?? process.env.OURA_ACCESS_TOKEN`). `syncFitbit` always reads from `user_integrations` and always persists rotated tokens via `persistRotatedToken` вҖ” profile-table read/write path deleted. Python scripts `sync-oura.py` and `sync-fitbit.py` updated identically; `update_env_token` helper and all `.env` write paths removed. `OURA_ACCESS_TOKEN` and `FITBIT_REFRESH_TOKEN` removed from both `web/.env.local.example` and root `.env.example`. **Post-deploy:** delete the `profile` row where `key = 'fitbit_refresh_token'` for the owner user.
- **`GOOGLE_REFRESH_TOKEN` retired from root `.env.example` + stale setup docs pruned (#393).** Follow-up to #396 which removed the runtime fallback. The root [.env.example](.env.example) still carried a "Migration fallback only" note for `GOOGLE_REFRESH_TOKEN`; replaced with a tombstone comment mirroring the `GOOGLE_FIT_*` retirement pattern. [README.md](README.md) file-tree annotation for `scripts/setup-web-oauth.py` updated to describe it as the legacy flow вҖ” per-user tokens now come from the `/settings вҶ’ Integrations` UI landed in #390. `OWNER_USER_ID` retained at line 68 and in README вҖ” still used by `/api/cron/sync` and the Python sync scripts. Closes #393.
- **`GOOGLE_REFRESH_TOKEN` / `OWNER_USER_ID` owner env fallback for Google auth (#396).** `getGoogleAuthClient` and `getGoogleAccessToken` now throw `GoogleNotConnectedError` unconditionally when `loadIntegration` returns null вҖ” no special-casing for the owner. The `/api/sync/googlefit` route similarly returns `{ skipped: true }` on no DB row without checking env vars. `GOOGLE_REFRESH_TOKEN` removed from `web/.env.local.example`; `OWNER_USER_ID` retained for cron sync only. Closes #396.
- `GOOGLE_FIT_REFRESH_TOKEN`, `GOOGLE_FIT_CLIENT_ID`, `GOOGLE_FIT_CLIENT_SECRET` env vars вҖ” superseded by `user_integrations` table.

### Changed
- **Token optimization вҖ” Claude Code context trimmed and .claudeignore added.** Monolithic `.claude/rules/mr-bridge-rules.md` (208 lines) split into `core.md` (always-loaded, 33 lines) + 7 on-demand files (`briefing.md`, `session-close.md`, `features.md`, `location.md`, `study-timer.md`, `voice.md`, `data-sources.md`). CLAUDE.md now imports `core.md` only; situational rules load via a pointer table when the relevant context is requested. Saves ~3,500вҖ“4,000 tokens of cold session context. `deepwiki` MCP removed from `.mcp.json` (unused). `.claudeignore` added covering build output, lock files, logs, secrets, and large generated files (CHANGELOG, renpho export).

### Added
- **CI вҖ” Smoke workflow with staged PR + nightly gates (#379).** Third Option-C follow-up from #373. New [.github/workflows/smoke.yml](.github/workflows/smoke.yml) with two jobs: **`smoke-pr`** runs `smoke:chat` + `smoke:a11y` on every pull_request that touches `web/**`, the smoke docs, `.mcp.json`, or the workflow file itself (paths-filtered to avoid churn on unrelated changes); **`smoke-release`** runs on a nightly `0 9 * * *` UTC cron plus `workflow_dispatch`, executes chat + a11y against Playwright-managed `next dev`, then stops dev / runs `next build` / starts `next start` / runs `smoke:perf` against the prod bundle / tears down. Playwright browsers cached with key `playwright-<runner>-<hash(package-lock.json)>` вҖ” `playwright install --with-deps chromium` fires only on cache miss. On failure both jobs upload `smoke/test-results/`, `smoke/playwright-report/`, and (release only) `smoke/perf-report/` as artifacts with 14-day retention. `concurrency.cancel-in-progress: true` scoped to `smoke-<workflow>-<ref>` so stale PR runs cancel on new pushes. Matches the [.github/workflows/lint.yml](.github/workflows/lint.yml) setup stanza (Node 20, npm cache on `web/package-lock.json`, `defaults.run.working-directory: web`, `npm ci`). **Required repo secrets** (set under Settings вҶ’ Secrets and variables вҶ’ Actions): `SMOKE_TEST_EMAIL`, `SMOKE_TEST_PASSWORD`, `SMOKE_SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY` (= `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`), `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY` (middleware hits this on every request), `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` (chat smoke hits Anthropic). Never scope any of them to production. The first run on this very PR will fail until the secrets land вҖ” that's expected, re-run the job from the Actions UI after adding them. [docs/smoke-testing.md](docs/smoke-testing.md) "CI" section rewritten (previously "Not yet configured"). Closes #379.
- **Calendar exclusion вҖ” per-profile `excluded_calendar_ids` to skip calendars across every Bridge read path (#388).** Motivated by #380: Jason created a dedicated smoke test Google Calendar under his own Google account, which auto-appears in his `calendarList` вҶ’ would leak test events into the briefing, the dashboard's Schedule Today widget, and the `list_calendar_events` chat tool. New helper at [web/src/lib/calendar/excluded.ts](web/src/lib/calendar/excluded.ts): `getExcludedCalendarIds(supabase, userId)` reads the `profile` row at `key = "excluded_calendar_ids"`, parses the JSON-array value, returns a `Set<string>`; fail-open on missing / malformed so a schema slip doesn't blank out the schedule. Three call sites now filter the `calendarList` result before fanning out `events.list`: [web/src/lib/tools/calendar.ts](web/src/lib/tools/calendar.ts) (chat tool вҖ” took `supabase` + `userId` from the existing `ToolContext`), [web/src/app/api/google/calendar/route.ts](web/src/app/api/google/calendar/route.ts) (dashboard Schedule Today widget), [web/src/app/api/google/calendar/upcoming-birthday/route.ts](web/src/app/api/google/calendar/upcoming-birthday/route.ts) (Upcoming Birthdays widget). No new migration needed вҖ” the `profile` table already has the key/value shape used by `sports_favorites` / `stock_watchlist` / etc. **Jason's profile needs one-time seeding** with the smoke calendar ID (documented in PR body). Closes #388.
- **Developer tooling вҖ” Lighthouse perf smoke across all 11 routes (#378).** Follow-up from #373's Option-C deferred scope; sibling to #377. New [web/smoke/perf/lighthouse.mts](web/smoke/perf/lighthouse.mts) runs the Lighthouse Node API against each route (mobile + desktop) three times and takes the median of CLS / LCP / TBT. **INP can't be measured in a lab run** (it's a field metric вҖ” requires real user interaction), so TBT is used as Google's published proxy per [web.dev/inp](https://web.dev/articles/inp). Thresholds from #323 Gate B: **CLS < 0.1**, **LCP < 2500 ms**, **TBT < 200 ms**. Auth for the 10 protected routes is solved via `chromium.launchPersistentContext()` with a user-data-dir: the script signs in via Playwright against that persistent Chrome (selectors mirror [smoke/fixtures/auth.ts](web/smoke/fixtures/auth.ts) вҖ” 8-line duplicate by design, since the fixture uses `test.extend` and doesn't fit a standalone script), and the new tab Lighthouse opens shares the same cookie jar. A short warm-up pass visits every route once after sign-in to pre-compile (no-op in prod, cuts first-audit LCP by 2вҖ“4 s in dev). The run is expensive (~7 min for 66 Lighthouse audits against a prod build) вҖ” intended for nightly / manual dispatch, not per-PR. New script `smoke:perf` in [web/package.json](web/package.json). New devDeps: `lighthouse`, `tsx` (the script is an ESM `.mts` because Lighthouse is ESM-only and the rest of the repo's TS config is CJS). Reports gitignored via [web/.gitignore](web/.gitignore) (`smoke/perf-report/`). **Per-route baselines at [web/smoke/perf/baselines.json](web/smoke/perf/baselines.json):** desktop passes all 11 routes cleanly against the prod build; mobile LCP fails on every route (3.0вҖ“4.2 s) and `/settings` mobile CLS fails at 0.163. Mobile LCP is a cross-cutting systemic issue (SSR'd client-component hydration cost under the mobile preset's 4Г— CPU throttle) and `/settings` mobile CLS is likely a mobile-only layout shift вҖ” both are too structural to fix in this PR. Baselined with +10 % tolerance for cold-run variance, tracked for ratchet-down in #384. The gate is `value вүӨ max(threshold, baseline)`, so today's known-bad routes don't block the pipeline but regressions past the current floor still fail. **Always run against `npm run build && npm run start` вҖ” never `next dev`.** Dev-mode Lighthouse mobile numbers are meaningless (dev has no minification, source maps on, HMR client wired up вҶ’ 6вҖ“10 s LCP floor regardless of real perf). [docs/smoke-testing.md](docs/smoke-testing.md) "What's covered today" and "Running locally" updated with the prod-build workflow and the baselines explanation. Closes #378.
- **Developer tooling вҖ” axe a11y smoke across all 11 routes (#377).** Follow-up from #373's Option-C deferred scope. New [web/smoke/specs/a11y.spec.ts](web/smoke/specs/a11y.spec.ts) data-drives `@axe-core/playwright` through `/dashboard`, `/chat`, `/fitness`, `/habits`, `/tasks`, `/weekly`, `/journal`, `/meals`, `/notifications`, `/settings`, `/login` вҖ” one `test()` per route so the HTML report carries per-route traces on failure. Reuses the `signedInPage` fixture from [web/smoke/fixtures/auth.ts](web/smoke/fixtures/auth.ts) for the 10 protected routes and a plain `page` for `/login`. Critical / Serious violations fail the test; Moderate / Minor findings surface as Playwright annotations via `testInfo.annotations.push({ type: "a11y:<impact>", ... })` so they accumulate in the report without blocking. Per-route settled signals are semantic (not `networkidle`, which never quiets on chat/dashboard due to streaming + polling): `<h1>` for the dashboard-like routes, `placeholder="Ask Mr. Bridge..."` for `/chat`, `getByLabel("Email")` for `/login`. New script `smoke:a11y` in [web/package.json](web/package.json) plus `@axe-core/playwright` devDep. Whole run is ~21s on a warm dev server, well under the 90s acceptance SLA. **Obvious critical findings fixed in the same PR:** missing `aria-label` on the chat composer `<textarea>` ([chat-interface.tsx:456](web/src/components/chat/chat-interface.tsx#L456) вҖ” `"Message Mr. Bridge"`), on two `<input type="date">` instances in tasks ([add-task-form.tsx](web/src/components/tasks/add-task-form.tsx), [task-item.tsx](web/src/components/tasks/task-item.tsx) вҖ” `"Due date"`), and on all four `<select>` meal-type pickers in [MealsClient.tsx](web/src/components/meals/MealsClient.tsx) вҖ” `"Meal type"`. **Baselined for design-token follow-up (#381):** the `color-contrast` rule is temporarily disabled via `.disableRules(["color-contrast"])` because every route fails it at the same three token surfaces вҖ” active nav link (`[aria-current="page"]`), segmented-control / tab / radio active button, and a small set of secondary-text spans. Re-enable when #381 lands. [docs/smoke-testing.md](docs/smoke-testing.md) "What's covered today" and "Running locally" updated. Closes #377.
- **Developer tooling вҖ” Playwright smoke infrastructure + Playwright MCP for interactive browser control (#373).** Automates the "start dev, sign in, send a chat, paste output back" loop that the manual chat-smoke rule covered вҖ” the rule caught PR #359, but skipping it caused the rollback in the first place. Two pieces land together per the issue's Option C: **(1) committed suite** at [web/smoke/](web/smoke/) with [playwright.config.ts](web/playwright.config.ts) (chromium, webServer auto-starts `next dev` on port 3000 with `reuseExistingServer` outside CI, trace + screenshot + video on failure, `fullyParallel: false` + `workers: 1` because specs touch a single shared test account), a signed-in page fixture at [smoke/fixtures/auth.ts](web/smoke/fixtures/auth.ts) that signs in via `getByLabel("Email")` / `getByLabel("Password")` / `getByRole("button", { name: "Sign in" })` and captures console errors + page errors through `page.on("console" | "pageerror")`, a service-role Supabase helper at [smoke/utils/supabase-verify.ts](web/smoke/utils/supabase-verify.ts) that bypasses RLS to query `chat_messages` for the test account, and the MVP spec at [smoke/specs/chat.spec.ts](web/smoke/specs/chat.spec.ts) вҖ” fills `getByPlaceholder("Ask Mr. Bridge...")` with `"what is 2+2"`, clicks `getByRole("button", { name: "Send" })`, races `page.waitForRequest` + `page.waitForResponse` + the click with `Promise.all`, reads the `sessionId` out of the POST body (session creation is lazy client-side via `crypto.randomUUID()`; server upserts `chat_sessions` on first POST), calls `chatResponse.finished()` so we wait for the stream body to close not just headers, asserts the assistant bubble is visible via the stable `data-print-message="assistant"` selector with matching `/4|four/i`, queries `chat_messages` for вүҘ 2 rows (user + assistant with non-empty `content`), and fails if any console error fired. Scripts added to [web/package.json](web/package.json): `smoke` (full suite), `smoke:chat`, `smoke:install` (one-time `playwright install --with-deps chromium`). Artifacts gitignored via [web/.gitignore](web/.gitignore) (`smoke/test-results/`, `smoke/playwright-report/`). **(2) Playwright MCP** вҖ” Microsoft's official [`@playwright/mcp`](https://github.com/microsoft/playwright-mcp) registered in [.mcp.json](.mcp.json) alongside the existing `deepwiki` entry, so Claude Code sessions in this repo surface `browser_navigate` / `browser_type` / `browser_click` / `browser_snapshot` tools and can drive a real browser during authoring and debugging. New env vars in [.env.example](.env.example): `SMOKE_TEST_EMAIL`, `SMOKE_TEST_PASSWORD`, `SMOKE_SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY` (aliased to the service-role key so the smoke code path is explicit). Full run-locally guide including the one-time Supabase-dashboard test-account creation lives at [docs/smoke-testing.md](docs/smoke-testing.md), with a short "Running smoke tests" section added to [README.md](README.md). **Deliberately out of scope for this PR** (filed as follow-up issues on merge per the Option C plan): axe a11y spec across 11 routes, Lighthouse perf runner with #323 thresholds, CI workflow with staged gates (`smoke:chat` + `smoke:a11y` per PR; `smoke:release` nightly), mutating-tool + multi-turn coverage (#319 false-success + #369 promise-to-continue). **Stays manual:** iOS Safari on real device, VoiceOver, Impeccable `/critique` + `/polish`, and any chat change not yet covered by a committed spec вҖ” the manual chat-smoke rule still applies there. Closes #373.
- **Anthropic extended thinking wired into the Sonnet chat path behind `ENABLE_THINKING` flag, default off (#339).** Measurement-first per the plan вҖ” the issue's three open decisions (enable at all? UX surface? per-model or global?) needed real data before committing to a UX. PR #350 cleared the way by collapsing the chat surface onto `ToolLoopAgent`, so the config now lives at the agent constructor in [web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts): `providerOptions: { anthropic: { thinking: { type: "adaptive" } } }` is spread onto `new ToolLoopAgent({...})` only when `modelTier === "sonnet" && process.env.ENABLE_THINKING === "1"` вҖ” Haiku and the Groq demo path receive nothing. **Adaptive mode, not enabled+budgetTokens** вҖ” per the @ai-sdk/anthropic docs, "for newer models (claude-sonnet-4-6, claude-opus-4-6, and later), use adaptive thinking" so the model self-selects whether each turn warrants reasoning. The existing `tokenBudgetExceeds(TOKEN_BUDGET = 150_000)` predicate in [route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts) covers reasoning automatically because Anthropic counts thinking as output tokens. Reasoning is **session-only** by three independent guarantees: (1) `sendReasoning: false` on `toUIMessageStreamResponse` вҖ” reasoning bytes don't cross the wire even though the SDK default is `true`; (2) the `chat_messages` insert path persists `text.trim()` only (or the #319 `synthesizeFallbackSummary` output when text is empty), neither of which can include reasoning since they're separate fields on the v6 `OnFinishEvent`; (3) the #319 synthesizer's input is `(steps, flags)` вҖ” reasoning isn't an addressable input, so it cannot substitute for a final answer. No client renderer changes; `getMessageText` in [chat-interface.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-interface.tsx) keeps filtering on `type === "text"`. **SDK finding** вҖ” `@ai-sdk/anthropic@3.0.0` does not break out reasoning into `outputTokens.reasoning` (always `undefined` per [convert-anthropic-messages-usage.ts](web/node_modules/@ai-sdk/anthropic/src/convert-anthropic-messages-usage.ts) lines 66вҖ“70 вҖ” Anthropic's API doesn't separately report reasoning_tokens in `usage`, the SDK just lumps everything into `outputTokens.total`). So usage-based accounting cannot tell us whether thinking fired. Instead `onFinish` reads `StepResult.reasoning` (an `Array<ReasoningPart>`) and `StepResult.reasoningText` directly вҖ” the only definitive signal вҖ” and the `[chat] cache ...` log line extends with three new key-value fields: `reasoningParts=<n>` (count of reasoning blocks across all steps), `reasoningChars=<n>` (sum of reasoning text length, a proxy for thinking volume since Anthropic bundles it into output token billing), and `thinkingEnabled=<true|false>` (the gate flag itself), so a baseline-vs-thinking A/B run is grep-able from one stdout file. **Measured A/B (5 prompts, Sonnet 4-6, real Bridge state, single-session-per-arm fallback after the new-chat-button hydration mismatch broke per-prompt fresh sessions):**

  | # | Prompt | Baseline ms | Thinking ms | О” ms | Baseline out tok | Thinking out tok | reasoningChars | Quality call |
  |---|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---|
  | 1 | `hi` | 1745 | 2093 | +348 | 12 | 42 | 51 | same |
  | 2 | Friday move + errands | 22177 | 24066 | +1889 | 586 | 1294 | 1746 | baseline (caught Giants game conflict, asked timing, offered Sunday) |
  | 3 | `move my workout` (ambig) | 8538 | 17278 | +8740 | 289 | 770 | 954 | thinking (flagged Giants game as timing constraint) |
  | 4 | deload swap | 20461 | 20553 | +92 | 596 | 1062 | 1289 | tied / baseline (better history narration + side-by-side table) |
  | 5 | meal Q&A | 14103 | 26888 | +12785 | 616 | 1430 | 2093 | **baseline (tool-use regression вҖ” thinking said "no saved recipes match" but baseline correctly found Air Fryer Chicken Thighs in saved recipes)** |

  **Aggregates:** mean latency baseline 13.4s вҶ’ thinking 18.2s (+4.8s, +36%); mean output tokens baseline 420 вҶ’ thinking 920 (+500, +119%); cost delta вүҲ +$7.50 per 1k turns at Sonnet's $15/MTok output rate (cache reads unchanged); reasoning fired on every turn including chitchat (adaptive mode is permissive, not selective). **Subjective:** baseline вүҘ thinking on 4 of 5 prompts, with one outright regression where thinking either skipped or misread the `get_recipes` tool. **Recommendation: do not enable by default.** The infrastructure (gate, adaptive provider config, reasoning instrumentation, sendReasoning gate, the SDK-extraction finding) ships behind `ENABLE_THINKING=0` so a future re-measurement can flip the flag вҖ” when a new Sonnet snapshot lands, when we want to evaluate Haiku, or when the prompt distribution shifts toward more multi-step planning. Out of scope and deferred unless future data justifies: a UX surface for reasoning (collapsed disclosure or "Bridge is thinkingвҖҰ" ambient strip extending #341), thinking on the Haiku path, swapping back to `enabled` mode with explicit `budgetTokens`, persisting reasoning to `chat_messages`, the per-prompt-conditional gate (route thinking only via the `selectModel` keyword/length predicates). Closes #339.

### Changed
- **Chat transport adopts `UIMessage.parts` end-to-end; chat history round-trips real tool calls and results (#342).** The v4вҶ’v6 SDK upgrade (#329) kept the legacy `{role, content: string}` wire shape via a `prepareSendMessagesRequest` shim in [web/src/components/chat/chat-interface.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-interface.tsx) вҖ” the minimal-diff path. Consequence: when the user reopened an old session, structured tool calls and results were a flattened text approximation, not the actual interaction. This PR keeps the structured shape across the whole boundary. **Schema** (new migration [supabase/migrations/20260420000000_chat_messages_add_parts.sql](supabase/migrations/20260420000000_chat_messages_add_parts.sql)): `chat_messages.parts jsonb NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]'`, backfilled from `content` as a single text part for every historical row. `chat_messages.content` stays `text NOT NULL` вҖ” it's the denormalized preview snapshot that the session-sidebar query at [web/src/app/api/chat/sessions/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/sessions/route.ts) keeps reading; explicitly not migrated to JSONB so the sidebar doesn't have to walk parts. RLS inherits automatically вҖ” the policy at [20260413000000_add_user_id_multitenancy.sql](supabase/migrations/20260413000000_add_user_id_multitenancy.sql) is row-scoped on `user_id`, no column whitelist. **Server** ([web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts)): POST accepts `UIMessage[]`, runs `convertToModelMessages` (the SDK already filters empty text parts, so the legacy empty-content guard is gone), and dual-writes both `parts` and `content` on every chat_messages insert. User-message persistence (pre-stream, the #132 durability path) writes `parts: lastUserMessage.parts` and the extracted text. Assistant-message persistence moved out of `ToolLoopAgent.onFinish` into `toUIMessageStreamResponse.onFinish` so it has access to the SDK's canonical `responseMessage.parts`; the bookkeeping (cache accounting, #319 synthesizer flag, #340 cache log line) stays in the agent's onFinish and stashes `contentToPersist` into a closure variable the outer onFinish reads. Reasoning parts are filtered before persist вҖ” #339 explicitly owns reasoning persistence and this PR keeps it ephemeral, matching the existing `sendReasoning: false` posture. **Client** ([web/src/app/(protected)/chat/page.tsx](web/src/app/\(protected\)/chat/page.tsx) + [web/src/components/chat/chat-page-client.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-page-client.tsx)): SSR loader + the four refetch paths (visibilitychange, loadSession, handleLoadMore, handleMessageSent) now hydrate UIMessages from the structured `parts` column; a `m.parts ?? [{type:'text', text: m.content}]` fallback covers any row missing parts (defensive against migration gaps; can be dropped in a follow-up cleanup PR once verified in production). Five identical inline mappers consolidated into a single `hydrateMessage` helper. **Transport** ([chat-interface.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-interface.tsx)): `prepareSendMessagesRequest` shim and its local `getMessageText` helper deleted вҖ” `DefaultChatTransport({ api: "/api/chat" })` now sends UIMessages directly. **Untouched (verified)**: session-sidebar preview query, `get_session_history` tool ([web/src/lib/tools/session.ts](web/src/lib/tools/session.ts)), the model-context loader at [route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts) which still reads `content` text (historical tool-result round-trips into the model context is a separate follow-up). The #319 synthesizer's text-to-`content` path is preserved exactly. **Verification**: `npm run build` clean, `npx tsc --noEmit` clean, `npm run lint` clean (0 / 0). Migration applied via `supabase db push`; smoke test against `npm run dev` covered the eight checks from the plan вҖ” fresh-session round-trip, multi-tool turn renders structured parts on reload (not synthesized paraphrase), forced tool failure preserved honestly per #319, #247 synthesized-fallback writes both columns, stop button (#352) preserves partial parts, pre-migration historical session renders identically, sidebar previews still read `content`, demo path (Groq) unchanged. Closes #342.
- **Chat agent surface refactored from hand-rolled `streamText` to v6 `ToolLoopAgent` (#350).** Follow-up to #337 once #340 (prompt caching) landed. [web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts) now instantiates a per-request `ToolLoopAgent({ model, instructions, tools, stopWhen, onFinish, prepareCall })` and invokes `agent.stream({ messages, abortSignal })`, replacing the `streamText(streamOptions)` call at the bottom of the route. Zero user-visible behaviour change вҖ” the route's four load-bearing contracts all survive unchanged: (1) **#319 verified-success** (`isToolResultOk` + `completedSteps` aggregation runs inside the new `onFinish`, which receives the identical `OnFinishEvent` shape as today), (2) **#346 habit-fabrication guard** (payload-side in [habits.ts](web/src/lib/tools/habits.ts), untouched), (3) **#247 deadline вҶ’ synthesized-fallback** (`synthesizeFallbackSummary` + its empty-text trigger still fire inside `onFinish`), (4) **#336 turn-complete sentinel** (stamped via `toUIMessageStreamResponse({ messageMetadata })` on `part.type === "finish"` вҖ” `messageMetadata` fires on both `start` and `finish` parts per [ai@6.0.168](web/node_modules/ai/dist/index.d.ts) line 2345). Field renamed `system` вҶ’ `instructions` per `ToolLoopAgentSettings`. `abortSignal` moved off the settings object (`ToolLoopAgent` omits it from the constructor) and passes through the per-call `.stream()` argument instead вҖ” the `turnAbort` AbortController + `TURN_DEADLINE_MS` wall-clock guard stay as-is, outside `stopWhen` because a step-boundary predicate cannot beat a Lambda kill mid-step. `onError` moved from the old `streamText` settings into `toUIMessageStreamResponse({ onError })`, which now returns the client-visible fallback string (`"An error occurred."`) matching the SDK's default. `prepareCall: async (args) => args` is a passthrough today but satisfies #350's stated contract that per-request tool factories wire through `prepareCall`; future non-streaming callers can reuse the same agent shape by swapping `.stream()` for `.generate()`. Type-only adjustment: `tokenBudgetExceeds` now carries a `<T extends ToolSet>` generic instead of the concrete `StopCondition<ToolSet>` return it had under `streamText`, because `ToolLoopAgentSettings.stopWhen` uses `StopCondition<NoInfer<TOOLS>>` and the SDK's own helpers (`stepCountIs`) return `StopCondition<any>` for the same reason вҖ” we parametrize instead to keep `--no-explicit-any` clean. Verification: `npm run lint` clean, `npm run build` clean, manual smoke test against `npm run dev` covered the seven checks from the plan вҖ” fresh session + tool call, multi-tool turn, mutating + confirmation with real calendar cross-check, forced tool error citing real state (#346 guard), `TURN_DEADLINE_MS` вҶ’ synthesized fallback, mid-stream stop button (#352 UI), `message.metadata.turnComplete` observable on the final assistant message. Out of scope and deferred: extended thinking (#339), non-streaming `.generate()` adoption (new follow-up filed, linked in PR). Closes #350.
- **Chat composer shows streaming tool state + stop button (#341, #352).** Two turn-in-flight UX wins shipped together. **#341:** [web/src/components/chat/tool-status-bar.tsx](web/src/components/chat/tool-status-bar.tsx) branched only on done-vs-not-done, so `input-streaming` and `input-available` rendered identically and `output-error` rendered with the green `вң“` (visual bug). The chip now reads all four AI SDK v6 states: `input-streaming` вҶ’ spinner + verb label (`"Looking up your calendarвҖҰ"`), `input-available` вҶ’ spinner + verb + safe argument preview (`"Looking up your calendar for Apr 18вҖҰ"`), `output-available` вҶ’ green `вң“` + faint text, `output-error` вҶ’ red `вң•` + `var(--color-danger)` border + `"${verb} failed"` copy. Argument preview is opt-in per tool via `TOOL_INPUT_PREVIEW` вҖ” the default is *no preview* so email queries, task content, journal entries, and meal-logging text never leak into the status bar. Whitelisted previews: `list_calendar_events` (date), `get_habits_today` / `get_fitness_summary` / `get_today_meals` / `get_workout_plan` / `get_workout_history` / `get_recipes` (date only if present), `get_stock_quote` (ticker), `get_sports_data` (team/league). Preview strings truncated to 25 chars. `TOOL_LABELS` extended from 13 to cover all 23 registered chat tools; stale `log_meal` entry removed (meals log via a separate route). **#352:** [web/src/components/chat/chat-interface.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-interface.tsx) now destructures `stop` from `useChat()` and the submit button swaps from `<Send>` to `<Square>` while `status === "streaming" || status === "submitted"` вҖ” same frame, border, and motion tokens, atomic `aria-label` swap ("Send" вҶ” "Stop generating"). Clicking the stop button calls `useChat()`'s `stop()`. A document-level `Escape` listener is attached only while a turn is in flight (textarea is disabled mid-stream so the per-textarea keydown can't fire) вҖ” triggers `stop()` with no effect on idle-composer `Esc` behaviour. No server changes вҖ” the abort lifecycle landed in earlier PRs (#247 `onFinish` fallback, #319 `turnComplete` sentinel, #337 abort signal plumbing). Partial transcript + `synthesizeFallbackSummary` already handle stopped-turn persistence correctly. Closes #341 and #352.
- **`react-hooks@7` rule set re-promoted to error (#363).** PR #362's Next 15вҶ’16 upgrade pulled in `eslint-plugin-react-hooks@7` via `eslint-config-next@16`, which adds four new rules (`set-state-in-effect`, `immutability`, `purity`, `refs`) as errors by default. #362 downgraded all four to `warn` to keep the upgrade's bisect surface minimal, leaving 15 pre-existing violations across 11 sites visible in lint output. This follow-up refactors every violation and removes the four rule overrides from [web/eslint.config.mjs](web/eslint.config.mjs) so Next 16's defaults take effect. No user-visible behaviour change expected вҖ” the rules become genuine enforcement instead of ignorable noise. Refactor shape by category: (a) `useSyncExternalStore` migrations for external-store reads вҖ” [web/src/lib/chart-colors.ts](web/src/lib/chart-colors.ts) (CSS variables via `MutationObserver` on `<html>`; also fixes the one-frame colour flash on theme toggle), `useReducedMotion` and touch-device detection in [web/src/components/charts/primitives.tsx](web/src/components/charts/primitives.tsx) + [web/src/components/chat/chat-interface.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-interface.tsx) (matchMedia), and three storage-backed reads in [web/src/components/chat/chat-page-client.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-page-client.tsx) (`chatHistoryOpen` in localStorage, `chatPrefill` in sessionStorage, hydration-safe via `getServerSnapshot`), plus the hydration `mounted` flag in [appearance-settings.tsx](web/src/components/settings/appearance-settings.tsx); (b) derive-during-render replacements вҖ” `granularity` in [activity-trends.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/activity-trends.tsx) now computes `forceWeekly ? "weekly" : userGranularity` each render instead of syncing via effect; (c) move setState out of synchronous effect body вҖ” [schedule-today.tsx](web/src/components/dashboard/schedule-today.tsx) shifts the `nowMinutes` set into the fetch `.finally()` alongside `setLoading(false)`, and [sports-settings.tsx](web/src/components/settings/sports-settings.tsx) hoists the "empty query" branch out of the debounce effect into the input's `onChange`; (d) immutability fixes вҖ” [meals/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/meals/page.tsx) rebuilds `macroTotals` in two immutable reduce passes (no more closure-variable mutation or post-reduce property reassignment), and [window-selector.tsx](web/src/components/ui/window-selector.tsx) moves the `document.cookie` write into a new `setWindowPreference` Server Action in [web/src/lib/window-actions.ts](web/src/lib/window-actions.ts) that calls `cookies().set()` + `revalidatePath("/", "layout")`, eliminating the `router.refresh()` call; (e) refs fix вҖ” drops the `activeSessionIdRef` latest-ref pattern in [chat-page-client.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-page-client.tsx), including `activeSessionId` in the visibility effect's dep array (cheap listener re-registration on session change) and in `handleMessageSent`'s `useCallback` deps (ChatInterface already re-keys per session, so `useChat` picks up fresh handlers); (f) purity fix вҖ” [notifications/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/notifications/page.tsx) wraps the Supabase fetch plus its `Date.now()` cutoff and in-band `read_at` update in a `cache()`-wrapped loader so the render body is just `await` + render. Vestigial-bug cleanup bundled in: removed the `sessionStorage` fallback effect for `activeSessionId` that was always overwritten by the persist-effect firing first in declaration order. Verification: `npm run lint` вҶ’ 0 errors / 0 warnings, `npx tsc --noEmit` clean, `npm run build` clean, dev-server smoke test covers chat mutating tools (#319 contract intact), theme toggle across dashboard/fitness/meals charts, meals delete, window-selector cookie, and notifications read-receipt flow.
- **Next.js 15.5.15 вҶ’ 16.2.4 (#328).** Major version bump, not a free upgrade вҖ” kept `ai`, Supabase, Tailwind, and Zod on their current majors to keep the bisect surface minimal if anything regresses. Four concrete breaking-change touches landed: (1) **`web/src/middleware.ts` вҶ’ `web/src/proxy.ts`** + function rename `middleware` вҶ’ `proxy`. Next 16 deprecated the `middleware` filename; `proxy.ts` runs on the Node runtime only (edge is unsupported), but Supabase SSR auth works identically on both, and the dev-server timing log confirms the rename is wired (`proxy.ts: 1806Вөs` appears per request). Verified end-to-end: `GET /` and `GET /dashboard` still redirect to `/login` when unauthed, `GET /login` returns 200. (2) **`next` + `eslint-config-next` bumped to `^16.2.4`** in [web/package.json](web/package.json); React resolved to `19.2.5` automatically via the existing `^19.1.0` range (Next 16's App Router uses the latest React canary). (3) **ESLint flat-config shim dropped.** Next 16's `eslint-config-next@16` ships a native flat config, so [web/eslint.config.mjs](web/eslint.config.mjs) was rewritten from `FlatCompat.extends("next/core-web-vitals", "next/typescript")` (the #327 pattern that wrapped the legacy Next 15 config) to direct imports: `import nextCoreWebVitals from "eslint-config-next/core-web-vitals"` + `import nextTypescript from "eslint-config-next/typescript"`. `@eslint/eslintrc@^3.3.5` removed from `devDependencies` вҖ” no longer referenced. This closes the follow-up #353 filed in #327. (4) **`react-hooks@7` new rules downgraded to `warn`.** The plugin bundled with Next 16 adds four new rules that error by default and surface 15 pre-existing violations in this repo: `react-hooks/set-state-in-effect`, `react-hooks/immutability`, `react-hooks/purity`, `react-hooks/refs`. Each flags a genuine React 19-era anti-pattern (mostly `useEffect вҶ’ setState` cascades in chart/theme hooks), but the violations are pre-existing behaviour and fixing them is not an upgrade task вҖ” filed as a follow-up. Downgrading to `warn` preserves the "lint stays green" contract from #327 without bundling ~15 hook refactors into this PR. Five rule entries added to [web/eslint.config.mjs](web/eslint.config.mjs) with the follow-up issue documented inline. **Non-hits verified absent** (would have forced code changes if present): no `revalidateTag` calls (only `revalidatePath`, unchanged), no `unstable_cacheLife`/`unstable_cacheTag`/`unstable_cache`, no `next/legacy/image`, no `images.domains` (new `minimumCacheTTL` 4h / `qualities: [75]` / `maximumRedirects: 3` defaults apply transparently, no custom `images` block to migrate), no parallel-route `@slot` directories, no `serverRuntimeConfig`/`publicRuntimeConfig`, no `experimental_ppr` or `dynamicIO`, no AMP, no `export const runtime = "edge"` in any route. Every `export const dynamic = "force-dynamic"` (10 protected pages) still works in 16 вҖ” no migration needed. Async Request APIs (`cookies`, `headers`, `params`, `searchParams`) already awaited everywhere per #319 work. **Turbopack is now the default for `next build`**; the repo has no custom webpack config so the build ran clean on first attempt (4.7s compile, 30 static pages, Next 16 surfaces the renamed proxy as `Ж’ Proxy (Middleware)` in the route list). **`web/tsconfig.json`** auto-updated by the first Next 16 build: `jsx` set to `"react-jsx"` (mandatory in 16), `.next/dev/types/**/*.ts` added to `include` (reflects the new concurrent dev/build output path вҖ” Next 16's `next dev` now outputs to `.next/dev` so `next build` and `next dev` can run concurrently). **[README.md](README.md)** updated: Claude Code CLI row bumped from "Requires Node 18+" to "Requires Node 20.9+ (Next.js 16 minimum)". Out of scope and deferred: PPR / `cacheComponents` adoption, the new `updateTag` / `refresh` / `cacheLife` / `revalidateTag(tag, profile)` caching APIs, React 19 Actions migration, React Compiler opt-in, Turbopack filesystem cache, Next DevTools MCP вҖ” each warrants its own issue. Verification: `npm run build` clean, `npx tsc --noEmit` clean, `npm run lint` clean (0 errors / 15 warnings from the downgraded react-hooks v7 rules), `npm run dev` starts in 204ms, proxy auth redirect verified via curl, HEAD/GET smoke tests green. Full UX walkthrough per [docs/audits/2026-04-17-pre-release.md](docs/audits/2026-04-17-pre-release.md) done manually pre-merge (dashboard + all widgets, chat stream with a mutating tool, settings save, habit check-in, journal save).
- **Anthropic prompt caching enabled on the chat route's static system prompt + tool schemas (#340).** Every chat turn to Anthropic was re-sending the full ~1.4k-token static system prompt and all 23 tool schemas as fresh input tokens, even though neither changes between turns within a session. v6 (PR #336) exposed `providerOptions.anthropic.cacheControl` but no route was using it. Two breakpoints now carry the cache вҖ” one on the last tool in the spread (caches every tool above it via Anthropic's "anchor the trailing block" semantics) and one on the static system message вҖ” leaving 2 of Anthropic's 4 allowed cache breakpoints unused. System prompt in [web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts) split from a single concatenated string into a two-entry `system` array: the static prefix carries `providerOptions.anthropic.cacheControl: { type: "ephemeral" }` (5-minute TTL), the dynamic block (today's date from `todayString()` + the user's name) follows uncached so turn-over-turn time drift doesn't invalidate the cache. Tool-side caching goes through a new `withTrailingCacheBreakpoint()` helper colocated with the tools spread, rather than edits across the 11 tool modules вҖ” a critical correction because Anthropic caps requests at 4 breakpoints and the SDK silently drops overflows; marking all 23 tool definitions would have exceeded the cap and left breakpoints past #4 un-cached, the same class of undocumented wire-limit trap that bit #343/#359/#360. Demo path (Groq) is gated out: the string `system` shape and unwrapped tools flow through unchanged. `onFinish` now emits a structured `[chat] cache ...` log line per turn carrying `inputTokens`, `outputTokens`, `cacheRead`, `cacheWrite`, `noCache`, and `warnings` (any `"cacheControl breakpoint limit"` or `"cache_control on non-cacheable context"` warning surfaces here so silent degradation doesn't hide). Budget-tracker semantics explicitly preserved: `usage.inputTokens` is the grand total processed by the model including cache reads and writes, so the existing `tokenBudgetExceeds(TOKEN_BUDGET = 150_000)` predicate in [route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts#L255-L272) still enforces the same ceiling вҖ” cache changes cost, not tokens-processed, and the ceiling protects against runaway context growth not dollar spend. A comment documents the invariant so it doesn't get "optimized" away later. **Measured delta** on a 2-turn real-user session (haiku, 2-step turns, tools invoked): turn 1 `inputTokens=13844, cacheRead=6448, cacheWrite=6448, noCache=948` вҖ” within-turn caching between the two model steps already firing; turn 2 `inputTokens=14088, cacheRead=12896, cacheWrite=0, noCache=1192` вҖ” steady-state, ~92% of input tokens served from cache at 10% cost. Effective per-turn input-token-equivalent cost drops from ~14k full-price to ~2.5k (`noCache + 0.1 Г— cacheRead`), roughly an 82% reduction on the input leg within the 5-minute cache window. `warnings=[]` on both turns; no Anthropic 400s observed; #319 verified-success contract and streaming behaviour unchanged. Local `npm run dev` smoke run performed before merge per the PR #360 process note. Out of scope for this PR and deliberately left untouched: system-prompt content edits, the pantry вҶ’ Supabase profile migration (still hardcoded in the cached prefix at line 167, memo'd separately), 1-hour cache TTL beta, and any caching on the Groq demo path.
- **Replaced deprecated `next lint` with ESLint CLI + flat config (#327).** `next lint` is removed in Next 16, and the existing `npm run lint` script was a no-op in non-interactive shells вҖ” it prompted the developer to pick a config and never returned a meaningful exit code, so CI had no actual lint enforcement and agent-driven edits flowed through an unchecked gate. Ran `npx @next/codemod@canary next-lint-to-eslint-cli .` to generate a flat-config `web/eslint.config.mjs`; the codemod's direct imports (`eslint-config-next/core-web-vitals`) don't run against `eslint-config-next@15` (which still ships legacy `.eslintrc`, not flat), so the config was rewritten to use `FlatCompat` from `@eslint/eslintrc` вҖ” the pattern Next itself documents for v15 + ESLint 9 (followup #353 to drop the shim once Next 16 lands). Rule set inherits `next/core-web-vitals` + `next/typescript` (pulls `@typescript-eslint`, `react-hooks`, `jsx-a11y`, `import` transitively). One project-convention override: `@typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars` with `argsIgnorePattern: "^_"` / `varsIgnorePattern: "^_"` вҖ” the codebase already uses the underscore-prefix convention (`_dt`, `_key`). CI wiring: [.github/workflows/lint-tokens.yml](.github/workflows/lint-tokens.yml) вҶ’ [.github/workflows/lint.yml](.github/workflows/lint.yml), now running two jobs (`lint-tokens` unchanged + new `eslint` job on Node 20 with npm cache scoped to `web/package-lock.json`). Ten violations fired on first run вҖ” all fixed rather than suppressed: two stale `eslint-disable-next-line` directives in [web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts) that were positioned on the wrong line (the `any` was on the next expression line, not the line after the comment) replaced with proper typing (`StopCondition<any>` вҶ’ `StopCondition<ToolSet>`; dropped `as any` on `streamOptions.model` вҖ” the `Parameters<typeof streamText>[0]` already accepts the model union); unused `fitnessRows` + its unused `fitness_log` Promise.all query removed from [dashboard/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/dashboard/page.tsx) (saves one Supabase round-trip per dashboard render); `_event` fix in [public/sw.js](web/public/sw.js); `postcss.config.mjs` switched from anonymous default export to named const; `aria-expanded` removed from the chat textarea ([chat-interface.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-interface.tsx)) вҖ” the attribute isn't supported on `role=textbox`; removed unnecessary `fetchSessions` from a `useCallback` dep array in [chat-page-client.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-page-client.tsx); dead `eslint-disable-next-line` deleted from [fitbit.ts](web/src/lib/sync/fitbit.ts). No behavioural change to the app. Follow-ups filed: #353 (drop FlatCompat after Next 16), #354 (pre-commit hook), #355 (Prettier evaluation), #356 (`@next/bundle-analyzer@^16` vs `next@^15` mismatch), #357 (fold `scripts/lint-tokens.sh` into ESLint as custom rule).

### Fixed
- **Strict mode disabled on all five mutating tools pending Anthropic compilation-limit investigation; schema tightenings kept (#343 rollback).** PR #359 enabled `strict: true` on five mutating tools (`create_calendar_event`, `update_calendar_event`, `assign_workout`, `update_workout_exercise`, `update_profile`) without first reproducing the full request path locally. Every chat request to Anthropic began failing with a 400, surfaced in the browser as the generic `Error вҖ” try again` banner on the first user message of every session. Local `npm run dev` would have caught it on the first turn; I skipped the smoke-start step from the plan, so the defect reached prod. Three distinct Anthropic strict-mode constraints surfaced in sequence as each one was addressed: (1) *every `object` schema must set `additionalProperties: false`* вҖ” fixed by adding the flag at every level across the five strict tools; (2) *total optional parameters across all strict tools вүӨ 24* (we were at 32; `assign_workout`'s 3 Г— 4-optional-per-item exercise arrays alone contribute 12, plus 5 top-level optional = 17) вҖ” addressed by dropping `assign_workout` from the strict set, bringing the remaining four to 15 optional; (3) *"schema is too complex for compilation"* вҖ” an undocumented ceiling that tripped even with the tightened four-tool set. Rather than iterate blind against a limit whose precise dimensions Anthropic doesn't document, all five `STRICT_TOOLS` flags are now `false` in [web/src/lib/tools/_strict.ts](web/src/lib/tools/_strict.ts), which restores the chat to working state. The schema tightenings stay вҖ” `additionalProperties: false` on every object schema, full `items` property shapes on `assign_workout.warmup/workout/cooldown` (previously `items: { type: "object" }` with no properties), and `additionalProperties: false` on `update_workout_exercise.updates`. These are correctness improvements regardless of strict mode. The `#319` `{ ok, error? }` runtime contract, read-after-write verifications, and calendar pre-flight rules are all unaffected and remain the primary defence. #343 is reopened with full repro context and the three observed Anthropic constraints; the next attempt will test the compilation budget empirically against one strict tool at a time before re-enabling across the mutating surface.
- **Chat reliability вҖ” `update_workout_exercise` error payload now cites real state, and five high-blast-radius mutating tools gate inputs at the provider boundary (#348, #343).** Two follow-ups on the #319 verified-success contract, shipped together. **#348:** the "not found" branch in [web/src/lib/tools/workouts.ts](web/src/lib/tools/workouts.ts) returned `Exercise "X" not found in warmup.` with no list of what *was* in the plan вҖ” the same defence-gap #346/#347 closed for `log_habit`. Now it lists the phase's real exercise names and directs the model: `"Current warmup exercises: A, B, C. Suggest one of these, or propose adding a new exercise вҖ” do not invent names."` Zero extra queries (the phase array is already in scope from the row fetch above). In practice the system prompt saves us because Bridge pre-calls `get_workout_plan`; this is the second-layer guard for long turns, post-compaction turns, and direct "change X to Y" instructions that skip the pre-check. **#343:** AI SDK v6 added `strict: true` on `tool({ ... })` which rejects malformed input shapes at the provider boundary before `execute()` runs. Enabled on the five tools where a bad input shape would corrupt user data: `create_calendar_event` + `update_calendar_event` ([web/src/lib/tools/calendar.ts](web/src/lib/tools/calendar.ts)), `assign_workout` + `update_workout_exercise` ([web/src/lib/tools/workouts.ts](web/src/lib/tools/workouts.ts)), and `update_profile` ([web/src/lib/tools/profile.ts](web/src/lib/tools/profile.ts)). Read-only tools and low-blast-radius mutations (`log_habit`, `add_task`, `complete_task`, `log_meal_from_scan`) are deliberately excluded per the issue вҖ” measure before enabling. Per-tool toggles live in a single new config module [web/src/lib/tools/_strict.ts](web/src/lib/tools/_strict.ts):
  ```ts
  export const STRICT_TOOLS = {
    create_calendar_event: true,
    update_calendar_event: true,
    assign_workout: true,
    update_workout_exercise: true,
    update_profile: true,
  } as const;
  ```
  Typed `as const` so any drift between the strict set and real tool names is a TS error at build time. The flag is an operational rollback lever вҖ” if a strict gate surfaces a latent schema narrowness under live traffic and Bridge starts refusing a valid intent, flip one entry to `false` and redeploy, no revert needed. If that happens in practice it's a follow-up to tighten the underlying schema, not a permanent override. Strict is additive to the #319 runtime contract: every affected tool still returns `{ ok, error? }` shapes for Supabase/Google failures; the new gate just moves shape-validation failures to the earliest possible layer.
- **`log_habit` `onConflict` target updated to match the multi-tenant unique constraint (#346).** Migration 20260417000001 (v1.1.0) rekeyed the `habits` unique constraint from `(habit_id, date)` to `(user_id, habit_id, date)` and updated [scripts/seed_demo.py](scripts/seed_demo.py) + [web/src/app/api/cron/reset-demo/route.ts](web/src/app/api/cron/reset-demo/route.ts) вҖ” but missed the chat tool's `log_habit` in the route. Every call was hitting `"no unique or exclusion constraint matching the ON CONFLICT specification"` and Bridge was interpreting the error as "habit already logged for today." Fix: update `onConflict: "habit_id,date"` вҶ’ `"user_id,habit_id,date"` in [web/src/lib/tools/habits.ts](web/src/lib/tools/habits.ts) вҖ” same change the other two call sites already had. Discovered during the fabrication-fix retest (same PR).
- **`log_habit` no longer lets the model fabricate alternative habits when the name doesn't match (#346).** When Bridge received a habit name that didn't exist, the tool returned an honest `{ ok: false, error: "No active habit matching ..." }` вҖ” but the model then invented plausible-sounding habits ("Morning Stretching, Evening Walk, Meditation...") that don't exist in the user's `habit_registry` instead of citing the real ones. A #319-class trust break, but in the **recovery-suggestion path** rather than the tool-return path вҖ” the tool was honest; the model hallucinated on top. Predated both PR #336 (v6 upgrade) and PR #345 (tool-module split) вҖ” reproduced identically on all three commits. Fix in [web/src/lib/tools/habits.ts](web/src/lib/tools/habits.ts): on lookup miss, query `habit_registry` for the user's actual active habit names and include them in the `error` string. The model then has concrete truth in context and has to directly contradict tool output to fabricate вҖ” in practice it cites the real list. Confirmed end-to-end on a fresh chat session (old sessions with the fabricated list cached in history will still regurgitate it вҖ” that's continuation bias, not a fix regression).

### Changed
- **Chat agent loop collapsed onto v6 composed `stopWhen` predicates (#337).** The step-cap and token-budget exits in [web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts) were wired through two different code paths вҖ” `stopWhen: stepCountIs(MAX_STEPS)` for steps, and a hand-tallied `cumulativeTokens` counter in `onStepFinish` that tripped the shared `turnAbort` AbortController when it crossed `TOKEN_BUDGET`. v6 lets `stopWhen` take an array of predicates composed with OR, so the budget check is now a pure `tokenBudgetExceeds(budget)` predicate sitting next to `stepCountIs(MAX_STEPS)`. Deleted: the `cumulativeTokens` / `budgetExceeded` hoisted `let`s and the entire `onStepFinish` callback (its only job was maintaining them). `onFinish` still surfaces `budgetExceeded` to `synthesizeFallbackSummary` and the diagnostic log line вҖ” it just reads it from a post-hoc reduction over `steps[].usage` instead of a live counter. `TURN_DEADLINE_MS` wall-clock guard untouched: it trips `turnAbort.abort()` mid-generation to beat Vercel's Lambda kill, which `stopWhen` predicates cannot do because they only evaluate between steps. Pure mechanical refactor вҖ” no user-visible change. The #319 verified-success contract, the #346 habit-fabrication guard, the #247 deadline вҶ’ synthesized-fallback path, and the #336 turn-complete sentinel on `message.metadata` all live outside loop mechanics and are structurally unaffected. Follow-up #350 filed to adopt `ToolLoopAgent` once #340 (prompt caching) and #339 (extended thinking) come online.
- **Meals routes migrated off deprecated `generateObject` (#338).** v6 kept `generateObject` functional but started emitting deprecation warnings in favour of `generateText({ output: Output.object({ schema }) })`. Four call sites under [web/src/app/api/meals/](web/src/app/api/meals/) switched to the new shape вҖ” [suggest/route.ts](web/src/app/api/meals/suggest/route.ts) (meal suggestions), [estimate-macros/route.ts](web/src/app/api/meals/estimate-macros/route.ts) (macro re-estimator), and the two branches in [analyze-photo/route.ts](web/src/app/api/meals/analyze-photo/route.ts) (food photo + nutrition-label modes). Models unchanged, vision inputs still use the v6 `mediaType` key from #336. Result destructured as `{ output }` instead of `{ object }`; the response shape the clients see is identical. **Schema tweak required:** `Output.object` forwards the ZodвҶ’JSON Schema output directly to Anthropic's native structured-output format, which is stricter than what `generateObject` was stripping вҖ” it rejects `minItems`/`maxItems` on arrays and the safe-integer `minimum`/`maximum` bounds Zod v4 emits for `.int()`. Surfaced at runtime as `output_config.format.schema: For 'вҖҰ' type, property 'вҖҰ' is not supported`. Minimal adjustment: dropped `.min(1).max(3)` from the `suggest` array (kept "2вҖ“3 meal suggestions (return between 1 and 3 items)" in the `.describe()` so the prompt still steers the model) and replaced `z.number().int()` with `z.number().describe("вҖҰ (integer)")` on six fields (`calories` Г—3, `sodium_mg` Г—2, label `calories` Г—1) across the three files. Lost validation is cosmetic вҖ” Claude returns integer calorie/sodium counts when told to; the prompt guidance was already doing the load-bearing work. Filed as a follow-up from PR #336 and closes the last of the v6-deprecation follow-ups for this PR's stack.
- **Chat tool definitions split out of `route.ts` into per-domain modules (#344).** The 23 `tool()` blocks that used to live inline in [web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts) вҖ” tasks, habits, fitness, profile, gmail, calendar, meals, session, workouts, stocks, sports вҖ” each now live in their own module under [web/src/lib/tools/](web/src/lib/tools/), exported as factory functions (`buildTasksTools(ctx)` etc.) that take a `ToolContext` ({ supabase, userId, isDemo, sessionId }) and return the tool object. Pure refactor, zero behaviour change; `route.ts` shrunk from 1954 lines to 576 (tool definitions: 1404 lines вҶ’ 0 inline). Shared: `web/src/lib/tools/_contract.ts` holds the `ok()` / `err()` helpers + `OkResult<T>` / `ErrResult` types (the #319 verified-success contract); `web/src/lib/tools/_context.ts` defines the per-request context. `isToolResultOk()` and `synthesizeFallbackSummary()` stay in `route.ts` because they're turn-orchestration concerns, not tool contract. Demo fixtures (`DEMO_EMAILS`, `DEMO_CALENDAR_EVENTS`) live in their respective tool modules; workout helpers (`WorkoutExercise`, `buildCalendarDescription`, `withTimeout`) live in [workouts.ts](web/src/lib/tools/workouts.ts).
- **Vercel AI SDK upgraded v4 вҶ’ v6 (#329).** Two-leg staged migration (4 вҶ’ 5, validated; 5 вҶ’ 6, validated). Dependency bumps: `ai@^4.3 вҶ’ ^6.0`, `@ai-sdk/anthropic@^1.2 вҶ’ ^3.0`, `@ai-sdk/groq@^1.2 вҶ’ ^3.0`, added `@ai-sdk/react@^3.0` (v5 moved `useChat` out of `ai/react`), `@ai-sdk/provider@^3.0`, `zod@^4.1.8`. No user-facing behaviour change; the rewrite is internal plumbing so future upgrades don't accumulate debt on top of #319's trickiest code. Key migrations: (a) `tool({ parameters })` вҶ’ `tool({ inputSchema })` across 24 tool definitions in [web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts) + [web/src/app/api/meals/scan-chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/meals/scan-chat/route.ts); (b) `maxSteps: N` вҶ’ `stopWhen: stepCountIs(N)`; (c) `LanguageModelV1Middleware` вҶ’ `LanguageModelV3Middleware` with `specificationVersion: "v3"` (import from `@ai-sdk/provider`); (d) `usage.promptTokens`/`completionTokens` вҶ’ `inputTokens`/`outputTokens` in the `onStepFinish` token-budget tracker; (e) tool result property `.result` вҶ’ `.output` in the onFinish step-pairing logic; (f) `StreamData` + `toDataStreamResponse({ data })` replaced with `toUIMessageStreamResponse({ messageMetadata })` вҖ” the #319 turn-complete sentinel now rides as metadata on the assistant message's finish part instead of a side-channel stream; (g) client-side `useChat` rewrite in [web/src/components/chat/chat-interface.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-interface.tsx) вҖ” v5 removed managed `input`/`handleInputChange`/`handleSubmit`/`isLoading`/`reload`, so the component now owns local input state, uses `DefaultChatTransport` with `prepareSendMessagesRequest` (flattens `UIMessage.parts` to the server's existing `{ role, content }` shape to avoid rewriting `/api/chat`'s message handling), and derives `isLoading` from `status`; (h) `Message` type replaced with `UIMessage` across 5 files вҖ” message content moved from `.content: string` to `.parts: Part[]`, `createdAt` moved into `message.metadata`; (i) `ToolStatusBar` updated for v5's per-tool UI part types (`tool-${name}` with `input-streaming`/`input-available`/`output-available`/`output-error` states); (j) `mimeType` вҶ’ `mediaType` on `ImagePart` in [web/src/app/api/meals/analyze-photo/route.ts](web/src/app/api/meals/analyze-photo/route.ts). Three new-capability items unlocked by the upgrade are filed as follow-up issues rather than bundled into this PR: `generateObject` вҶ’ `generateText({ output })` migration (4 call sites in meals routes, deprecated in v6 but functional), `stopWhen` / `ToolLoopAgent` refactor of the manual step-cap + synthesizer logic in the chat route, and Anthropic prompt caching on the system prompt + tool definitions.

### Fixed
- **Upcoming-birthday widget no longer doubles the "birthday" suffix (#334).** When a Google Calendar event title ended in trailing text after `'s birthday` вҖ” e.g. `Albert Autin's Birthday рҹҺҲ` вҖ” the widget rendered *"Albert Autin's Birthday рҹҺҲ's birthday"* because the `/'s birthday$/i` anchor failed on the trailing emoji and `personName()` returned the title unchanged, leaving the JSX template to append the suffix on top of the one already in the title. Switched the detector to `/'s birthday\b/i` (word boundary) and the stripper to `/'s birthday.*$/i` in [web/src/app/api/google/calendar/upcoming-birthday/route.ts](web/src/app/api/google/calendar/upcoming-birthday/route.ts); applied the same boundary change to the `isBirthday` flag in [web/src/app/api/google/calendar/route.ts](web/src/app/api/google/calendar/route.ts) so the main agenda view agrees with the widget on what counts as a birthday event.
- **Demo account no longer pulls real contacts' birthdays (#334).** The upcoming-birthday route had no `DEMO_USER_ID` gate (unlike the main calendar route), so demo visitors were reading birthdays from the owner's Google Calendar. Added a short-circuit that returns a fixed fake persona вҖ” Priya, already the demo user's lunch-buddy in [web/src/app/api/google/calendar/route.ts](web/src/app/api/google/calendar/route.ts)'s mock events вҖ” with `daysUntil: 12` and a date computed dynamically in `USER_TZ` so the widget is always populated on the demo dashboard without hitting Google.

### Added
- **Delete a logged meal (#330).** Each row in *Logged Today* and *Past 6 Days* now has a trash icon. Tap вҶ’ row disappears immediately and today's macro totals (calories, protein, carbs, fat, fiber, sugar) recompute from the visible rows; a 5-second "Meal deleted" undo toast lets the user restore the row before commit. After the toast expires, `DELETE /api/meals/log` fires; if the user navigates away inside the window, an unmount cleanup flushes the pending delete via `fetch(..., { keepalive: true })` so it leaves the browser even as the page tears down. New `DELETE` handler on [web/src/app/api/meals/log/route.ts](web/src/app/api/meals/log/route.ts) is user-scoped (`createClient()` + `eq("user_id", user.id)` + 404 on cross-user IDs). Reuses the [`UndoToastProvider`](web/src/components/ui/undo-toast.tsx) built for chat session deletion (#205); macro totals are recomputed client-side via a small helper in [MealsClient.tsx](web/src/components/meals/MealsClient.tsx) that mirrors the SSR reduce in [page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/meals/page.tsx). The dedupe-driven *Recent meals* row is intentionally excluded вҖ” those are historical references for re-logging, not the source rows themselves; deleting them would be ambiguous.

## [1.1.0] вҖ” 2026-04-17

First minor release after v1.0.0. Headliners: the #319 verified-success contract across every mutating chat tool (Bridge no longer claims an action succeeded when the underlying tool returned an error or the Lambda died mid-stream); the Phase B Impeccable UI revamp landing Weekly, Meals, Notifications, Settings, and Login on the dashboard-panel pattern; macro editing with fiber + sugar tracking and Bridge chat-logging of food-photo scans (#302/#303/#304); habits momentum line and longest-chain badges (#317); and the refreshed demo account (#251). Pre-release audit (#252) closed the cut with no critical or high findings вҖ” see [docs/audits/2026-04-17-pre-release.md](docs/audits/2026-04-17-pre-release.md).

### Fixed (pre-release audit trivial fixes, issue #252)
- **`.env.example` Supabase variable names corrected.** The file was documenting `SUPABASE_URL` / `SUPABASE_ANON_KEY`, but every call site in [web/src/lib/supabase/client.ts](web/src/lib/supabase/client.ts), [web/src/lib/supabase/server.ts](web/src/lib/supabase/server.ts), [web/src/lib/supabase/service.ts](web/src/lib/supabase/service.ts), [web/src/middleware.ts](web/src/middleware.ts), and [web/src/app/auth/callback/route.ts](web/src/app/auth/callback/route.ts) reads `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL` / `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY`. A fresh clone using the documented names would fail to boot. Primary keys are now prefixed; the unprefixed `SUPABASE_URL` is retained with a comment explaining it's for the Python scripts under `scripts/`, which don't read `NEXT_PUBLIC_*`.
- **`.env.example` now documents nine previously-missing env vars** referenced in code but absent from the template: `POLYGON_API_KEY` (stocks widget), `SPORTSDB_API_KEY` / `SPORTS_PROVIDER` (sports widget), `GROQ_API_KEY` (chat "fast" model path), `USER_TIMEZONE` (date-window helpers), `CRON_SECRET` + `OWNER_USER_ID` (Vercel cron endpoints under `/api/cron/*`), and `GOOGLE_FIT_CLIENT_ID` / `GOOGLE_FIT_CLIENT_SECRET` (optional Fit-specific OAuth credentials when separate from Calendar/Gmail).
