- **[README.md](README.md): "all 20 tables" вҶ’ "all tables"** вҖ” the count (21 with `strength_session_sets`) was out of date; removed the number instead of bumping it so it stops going stale on every schema migration. `sports_cache` added to the example list.
- **[.claude/rules/mr-bridge-rules.md](.claude/rules/mr-bridge-rules.md): dropped the "(future)" Web UI hook note.** Referenced issue #10 ("when the web interface is built") вҖ” but the web interface has shipped and `/settings` exposes the Location field today. Removed rather than rewritten because the guidance is now documented behaviour, not a forward instruction.
- **Audit report committed** at [docs/audits/2026-04-17-pre-release.md](docs/audits/2026-04-17-pre-release.md) with go/no-go recommendation and follow-up findings filed as separate issues.

### Changed (demo account refresh вҖ” release prep, issue #251)
- **Demo persona renamed "Alex / Alex Chen" вҶ’ "Demo User"** across the two profile rows seeded by [scripts/seed_demo.py](scripts/seed_demo.py) and [web/src/app/api/cron/reset-demo/route.ts](web/src/app/api/cron/reset-demo/route.ts), plus the chat route's fallback label and demo system prompt in [web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts). Visitors kept reading "Alex" in the briefing as a real teammate's note; "Demo User" is unambiguous. Gmail / Calendar mock-content names in [web/src/app/api/google/gmail/route.ts](web/src/app/api/google/gmail/route.ts) + [web/src/app/api/google/calendar/route.ts](web/src/app/api/google/calendar/route.ts) are intentionally preserved вҖ” they're realistic sample-content inside demo fixtures, not the demo user's identity.
- **Seed extended to cover four surfaces that shipped since the last refresh.** [scripts/seed_demo.py](scripts/seed_demo.py) now populates `chat_sessions` + `chat_messages` (3 sample conversations: post-workout meal Q&A, calendar scheduling, workout tweak), `stocks_cache` (AAPL / NVDA / MSFT with recent quotes + 20-point sparklines), `sports_cache` (Warriors / 49ers / Earthquakes with recent game state), and `strength_sessions` + `strength_session_sets` (6 lifting sessions over 3 weeks to fill the #249 progression visuals). Every row is written with `user_id = DEMO_USER_ID` explicitly вҖ” no OWNER_USER_ID path, no implicit default (#133 regression gate). `seed_meal_log` now includes `sugar_g` (#304).
- **Meal-log seed is idempotent.** `seed_meal_log` switched from `.insert()` to `.upsert(on_conflict="user_id,date,meal_type,recipe_id")`. Re-running `scripts/seed_demo.py` no longer duplicates ~40 meal rows per run.
- **`scripts/reset_demo.py` TABLES list extended** to wipe `strength_sessions`, `stocks_cache`, and `sports_cache`. `strength_session_sets` is cascaded via the parent `strength_sessions` FK rather than listed directly (it has no `user_id` column вҖ” scoping flows through the parent session's RLS subquery per migration `20260416000000`).
- **`README.md` + `.env.example` document the re-run flow.** New "Refreshing the demo account between releases" section with both `reset_demo.py` and `seed_demo.py` entry points, the OAuth manual-relink list (Google Calendar + Gmail, Oura, Fitbit, Google Fit), and a heads-up that the new migration (20260417000001) must be applied before re-running. `.env.example` now documents `DEMO_USER_ID`, `DEMO_EMAIL`, `DEMO_PASSWORD`, and the two `NEXT_PUBLIC_*` variants.

### Fixed (multi-tenant unique constraint gaps вҖ” latent #133-class hazards, issue #251)
- **`habits` unique constraint rekeyed `(habit_id, date)` вҶ’ `(user_id, habit_id, date)`** in migration [supabase/migrations/20260417000001_fix_multitenant_unique_constraints.sql](supabase/migrations/20260417000001_fix_multitenant_unique_constraints.sql). The original key only pulled `user_id` in through `habit_id`'s FK to `habit_registry`; the explicit `user_id` in the key is what the `onConflict` upsert target in [scripts/seed_demo.py](scripts/seed_demo.py) + [web/src/app/api/cron/reset-demo/route.ts](web/src/app/api/cron/reset-demo/route.ts) needs to address an upsert unambiguously. Both call sites updated to the new target.
- **`meal_log` gained a unique constraint `(user_id, date, meal_type, recipe_id)`** вҖ” the table previously had none, so seeding inserted duplicate rows on each re-run. `recipe_id` is nullable and Postgres treats NULLs as distinct, which is the correct semantics here: ad-hoc meals on the same day/meal_type (e.g. two snack entries for a double-lunch) don't collide, but the saved-recipe meals do upsert cleanly.

### Fixed (chat вҖ” verified-success contract for mutating tools, issue #319; supersedes #223)
- **Canonical `{ ok, error? }` shape on every state-mutating chat tool** in [web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts). New `ok()` / `err()` helpers wrap the return values of `add_task`, `complete_task`, `log_habit`, `update_profile`, `create_calendar_event`, `update_calendar_event`, `delete_calendar_event`, `assign_workout`, and `update_workout_exercise`. Previously each tool used a different shape on success (`{ updated: true }`, `{ deleted: true }`, raw row, `{ written: [...] }`) and `{ error: ... }` on failure вҖ” so the model and the fallback synthesizer could not reliably distinguish "the action happened" from "the action didn't happen", which let Bridge claim a calendar move had succeeded when the underlying tool result was a hallucination. Every Supabase write now also null-checks the returned row and returns an error if zero rows landed (closes the silent-`.single()`-returns-null class).
- **Read-after-write verification on calendar mutations** for `create_calendar_event`, `update_calendar_event`, and `delete_calendar_event`. After Google's response we issue an `events.get` and confirm the resulting `start` / `end` / `summary` / `location` (or `status === "cancelled"` for delete) match the requested change. Mismatches return `ok: false` with a specific error so Bridge tells the user instead of falsely confirming. The same pattern is applied inline to `update_workout_exercise` (re-reads the workout plan row and confirms the matched exercise's fields contain the requested updates) вҖ” addresses the parallel #239 false-success class.
- **Synthesizer fallback inspects tool results, not just tool calls.** `synthesizeFallbackSummary` now pairs each `toolCall` with its `toolResult` via `toolCallId`, splits into `succeeded` / `failed`, and emits one of three branches: "Done. I {phrases}." / "I tried to {phrases} but it didn't go through вҖ” {error}. Please try again." / "Partial: I {ok phrases}, but failed to {failed phrases} ({first error}). Check before retrying." This was the structural defect that let PR #247's fallback emit "Done. I updated a calendar event." for a tool that had returned an error.
- **System-prompt verified-success rule** added to `STATIC_SYSTEM_PROMPT`: "Never say a mutating action is 'done' or use вң“ unless the most recent tool result for that action has `ok: true` in this turn. If you don't see a successful tool result, either run the tool now or tell the user the action didn't go through." Last-line-of-defense complement to the structural fixes above.
- **Per-turn deadline guard so `onFinish` always runs.** New `TURN_DEADLINE_MS = 80_000` and `maxDuration` raised 60 вҶ’ 90 seconds. The deadline timer aborts the agent loop ~10s before Vercel's hard kill so `onFinish` always fires, persists a fallback assistant message, and emits the SSE turn-complete frame вҖ” the exact silent-stall path that hit on issue #319's repro session, where the Lambda died mid-stream and PR #247's fallback never got the chance to run. Completion log now also reports `deadlineExceeded` and `toolFailures=N/M`.
- **SSE turn-complete sentinel** emitted via `StreamData` from `onFinish`. The client-side `useChat` reads `data` for a `{ type: "turn-complete" }` frame; if absent when the stream ends вҖ” i.e. the Lambda was killed without `onFinish` running, or the network cut the SSE early вҖ” the parent ([web/src/components/chat/chat-page-client.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-page-client.tsx) `handleMessageSent`) refetches the active session from the server. The server-persisted assistant message (verified-success or fallback) becomes the source of truth, replacing whatever partial state useChat held locally.
- **Context loader off-by-direction fixed.** [web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts) was loading the FIRST 10 messages of a session for context (`order ascending + limit 10`); for any session past 10 turns the model lost recent context including its own prior tool results, which made the bug-1 hallucination easier. Now loads the last 10 (`order descending + limit 10` then `.reverse()`).
- **Diagnosis evidence in PR description.** chat_messages for the repro session showed no assistant row persisted between user "Yes please" and user "Did you finish?" вҖ” confirming PR #247's `onFinish` never ran. The next turn's "Yes, done!" message was generated in 3 seconds with no tool call (proven by row timestamps and the absent assistant-row gap), and the user manually moved the calendar event afterward.

### Fixed (Gate B audit follow-ups вҖ” Impeccable revamp, issue #272)
- **Dashboard Recharts dependency dropped** in [web/src/components/dashboard/watchlist-widget.tsx](web/src/components/dashboard/watchlist-widget.tsx). The ticker sparkline was the sole remaining Recharts consumer. Replaced `<LineChart>` + `<Line>` + `<ResponsiveContainer>` with a local `Sparkline` component (~30 lines) emitting a single `<path>` inside a responsive SVG (`viewBox="0 0 100 20"` + `preserveAspectRatio="none"` + `vectorEffect="non-scaling-stroke"` to keep the 1.5px stroke crisp as the row width flexes). `recharts` removed from [web/package.json](web/package.json). **`/dashboard` first-load JS: 220 kB вҶ’ 121 kB** (вҲ’99 kB). All 11 routes now sit under the 200 kB Lighthouse threshold.
- **Motion-token drift retired across eight call sites.** Replaced `transition-all duration-150/200/300` + `transition-colors duration-150` Tailwind classes with explicit `transition: ... var(--motion-fast|base|slow) var(--ease-out-quart)` inline styles in: [theme-toggle.tsx](web/src/components/theme-toggle.tsx), [ui/sign-out-button.tsx](web/src/components/ui/sign-out-button.tsx), [ui/metric-card.tsx](web/src/components/ui/metric-card.tsx), [meals/MacroSummaryCard.tsx](web/src/components/meals/MacroSummaryCard.tsx) (2Г—), [meals/MealsClient.tsx](web/src/components/meals/MealsClient.tsx) (2Г—), and [meals/FoodPhotoAnalyzer.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/meals/FoodPhotoAnalyzer.tsx). The proposal's "zero `duration-NNN` in revamped components" rule now holds across the entire web tree.
- **Progress-bar fill switched from width animation to transform** in [meals/MacroSummaryCard.tsx](web/src/components/meals/MacroSummaryCard.tsx) + [meals/MealsClient.tsx](web/src/components/meals/MealsClient.tsx). The former `width: {pct}%` with a `transition: width` animated a layout property вҖ” cheap to implement, expensive at paint time and now flagged by Impeccable's `layout-transition` antipattern. Rewrote as a full-width child with `transform: scaleX({pct}/100)` + `transform-origin: left center` + `transition: transform`. Same visual, GPU-compositable, no layout thrash.
- **Impeccable detector clean** вҖ” `docs/design/impeccable-revamp/impeccable-detect-post-phase-b.json` now reports `[]` (0 antipatterns). Baseline was 6; post-Phase-A was 4; post-Phase-B pre-audit was 0; a regression was introduced + caught + fixed while retokenizing the progress bar motion; final snapshot is clean.
- **Gate B audit report** committed at [docs/design/impeccable-revamp/audit-final.md](docs/design/impeccable-revamp/audit-final.md) вҖ” mechanically-verified dimensions (build, detector, bundle thresholds, token adoption, dead-code removal, grep sweep) all pass; manual dimensions (axe, Lighthouse, VoiceOver, cross-browser, responsive, regression smoke) flagged for pre-ship human verification.

### Added (Food Analyzer + Meals вҖ” editable macros, Bridge chat logging, fiber + sugar tracking В· issues #302 #303 #304)
- **Inline-editable macros in the analyzer review panel (#302)** in [web/src/app/(protected)/meals/FoodPhotoAnalyzer.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/meals/FoodPhotoAnalyzer.tsx). Calories / protein / carbs / fat / fiber / sugar now render as six controlled numeric inputs inside the Edit expand panel for every scan item (label-mode scans are now editable too вҖ” previously only food-mode with ingredients could expand). Each field carries a per-field `*ManuallyEdited` flag on `ScanItem`; re-estimate merges field-by-field so editing calories doesn't freeze out a sugar re-estimate and vice versa. A new `MacroInput` helper keeps a local text buffer synced to the external numeric value via a ref, so re-estimate can refresh AI-only fields without fighting the controlled input during user typing.
- **Soft calorie-consistency warning pill (#302)** non-blocking. Rendered inside the same expand panel using `--color-danger-subtle` background + `AlertCircle` when `abs(userCals - (protein*4 + carbs*4 + fat*9)) / derivedCals > 0.10`. Copy surfaces the derived kcal and a "You can log anyway" hint вҖ” user can save through the soft guardrail.
- **Bridge logs meals from the inline analyzer chat (#303)** via a new scoped endpoint [web/src/app/api/meals/scan-chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/meals/scan-chat/route.ts). Registers exactly one tool вҖ” `log_meal_from_scan` вҖ” that does NOT write to the DB; it returns a structured `log_meal_proposal` payload which the client renders as an action card with `[Log]` / `[Cancel]` buttons. The DB write only happens after the user confirms. General `/api/chat` remains tool-free for meal logging so Bridge cannot log meals outside the analyzer context (explicit #303 scoping decision).
- **Propose вҶ’ confirm action card rendering** in rewritten [web/src/app/(protected)/meals/InlineMealChat.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/meals/InlineMealChat.tsx). `ChatMessage` type now discriminates `text` vs `proposal` entries. Stream parser consumes both AI-SDK prefixes (`0:` text, `a:` tool result) line-by-line with a rolling buffer. Confirm calls `/api/meals/log` with the proposal's totals, shows a "Logged вң“" state, and fires an `onLoggedViaChat` callback on the parent вҖ” which clears scan items so no double-log is possible. Adjustment flow works conversationally: "add extra rice" вҶ’ Bridge recomputes macros and re-proposes, user confirms a single final card.
- **Fiber + sugar tracked per meal (#304)** вҖ” new migration [supabase/migrations/20260417000000_add_sugar_to_meal_log.sql](supabase/migrations/20260417000000_add_sugar_to_meal_log.sql) adds `sugar_g numeric(6,1)` to `meal_log` (fiber_g was already present from migration 20260412000000 but was not surfaced in the analyzer's log payload вҖ” this PR fixes that dropout too). Both columns remain nullable; legacy rows render as `вҖ”` in the UI, never `0`.
- **Estimate-macros + analyze-photo schemas extended** in [web/src/app/api/meals/estimate-macros/route.ts](web/src/app/api/meals/estimate-macros/route.ts) + [web/src/app/api/meals/analyze-photo/route.ts](web/src/app/api/meals/analyze-photo/route.ts). Both `MacroEstimateSchema` and `FoodAnalysisSchema` now include `sugar_g: z.number().nullable()` and fiber_g is relaxed to nullable as well вҖ” the model is allowed to return null for foods that legitimately lack a nutrient (butter has no fiber, plain meat has no sugar) instead of being forced to invent a 0.
- **`/api/meals/log` accepts + writes `sugar_g`** on POST and PATCH; PATCH also now accepts `fiber_g` (was silently dropped before). [web/src/app/api/meals/log/route.ts](web/src/app/api/meals/log/route.ts).
- **Daily fiber bar + sugar running-total on the Meals tab (#304)** in [web/src/components/meals/MealsClient.tsx](web/src/components/meals/MealsClient.tsx). Fifth `MacroBar` renders under the four macro bars using the existing component, goal pulls from `profile.fiber_goal` and defaults to 30g when unset (applied in [web/src/app/(protected)/meals/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/meals/page.tsx)). Sugar renders below as a new hairline-separated `SugarTotalRow` вҖ” total-only, no bar, matching the #304 decision that sugar is awareness-oriented, not target-oriented. Null totals render as `вҖ”`.
- **Logged-meal rows surface fiber + sugar** on expanded-row display in `MealRowDisplay` via new `formatNutrientCol` helper. `MealRowEdit` grows a second row of inputs for `fiber_g` + `sugar_g` with explicit null-preservation вҖ” blank field in the editor clears the DB value to NULL rather than coercing to 0. Both TodayTab and PastMeals edit paths updated. A shared `MealRowEditFields` interface replaces the duplicated inline type.
- **Server-side `MacroTotals` + `MacroGoals` extended** to carry `fiber` / `sugar` (null-aware) and `fiber` goal respectively. Today's totals computation walks meals once, tracking per-nutrient `any` flags so fiber/sugar stay null when nothing today reports them.
- **Scan вҶ” chat sync** вҖ” `FoodPhotoAnalyzer` passes `items`, the current `logMealType`, and an `onLoggedViaChat` callback down to `InlineMealChat`. The callback calls `clearAll()` + `router.refresh()` after the chat-initiated log lands, keeping the analyzer scan panel and chat state consistent (no double-log window).
- **Combined-totals row shows fiber + sugar** below the existing combined macro line when at least one scanned item reports those nutrients. Uses a new `sumNullable` helper + `roundOrDash` to preserve the null-as-`вҖ”` contract from individual items through aggregates.
- **Scanner-logged `fiber_g` no longer silently dropped.** Previously `/api/meals/log` accepted `fiber_g` but the analyzer's log payload never included it, so `meal_log.fiber_g` was NULL for every scanner-sourced row. This PR sends `fiber_g` + `sugar_g` on both the standard log path and the meal-prep split path (scaled by servings / container count with the same rounding as the four basic macros).
- **Tokens-only styling.** Every new surface uses `--color-*` / `--rule*` / `--space-*` / `--t-*` / `--r-*` / `--motion-*` tokens; no Tailwind color classes were introduced.
- **Type-checked + built.** `npx tsc --noEmit` clean; `next build` succeeds with the new `/api/meals/scan-chat` route visible in the route table.

### Changed (Habits вҖ” momentum line + longest-chain badges, issue #317)
- **Completion heatmap retired** in [web/src/app/(protected)/habits/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/habits/page.tsx). The 14-to-365-day grid of light/dark squares is replaced by the two visualizations below вҖ” at five active habits the heatmap was visually sparse and answered the wrong question ("which day did I miss?") instead of the trend question the user actually has ("am I getting better?"). Deleted: [web/src/components/habits/heatmap.tsx](web/src/components/habits/heatmap.tsx).
- **Momentum line shipped** in new [web/src/components/habits/momentum-line.tsx](web/src/components/habits/momentum-line.tsx). Renders the 30-day rolling 7-day completion rate across all active habits (denominator = `habits.length Г— 7`, matching the Weekly Completion radial). Reuses the shared `TrendLine` + `ChartFrame` + `EndpointLabels` primitives вҖ” no new SVG. Today marked with a 3px `--accent` dot + 6px halo per Phase A vocabulary; dashed 1px `--chart-color-baseline` reference line at the trailing 30-day average; hover readout uses the hairline-pill treatment (`--color-surface-raised` + `--rule` border) that the fitness + health-breakdown surfaces already use. Endpoint labels render "Mar 18" / "Today" via the existing `EndpointLabels` helper. `yDomain` clamped to `[0, 100]` so the chart scale reads as completion %.
- **Empty state** for the momentum line when fewer than 7 distinct completed-log dates exist in the 30-day window вҖ” renders "Not enough history yet вҖ” 7 days of logs needed to show momentum." in `--t-body` / `--color-text-faint` inside the chart frame, no broken line.
- **Per-habit longest-chain badges shipped** in new [web/src/components/habits/longest-chain-badges.tsx](web/src/components/habits/longest-chain-badges.tsx). Renders a `db-row`-vocabulary list: habit name on the left at `--t-body`, tabular `{current}d В· best {best}d` on the right (current weight 500 `--color-text`, best `--color-text-faint`). Rows sorted by current streak desc, ties broken by `name.localeCompare`. Hairline-separated, 44px min-height, no card shell.
- **Personal-best accent pip** fires only when `current === best && current > 0` вҖ” a 6px `--accent` circle next to the current-streak number. Hidden the rest of the time so the accent keeps its "rarity gives it power" rule.
- **`StreakChart` retired** in favor of the longest-chain badge rows вҖ” the horizontal-bar component rendered the same per-habit numbers as the new rows (plus a bar no one needed) and duplicated the data. Deleted: [web/src/components/habits/streak-chart.tsx](web/src/components/habits/streak-chart.tsx).
- **`computeStreaks` reused as-is** вҖ” the helper in [web/src/lib/streaks.ts](web/src/lib/streaks.ts) already returns `{ current, best }` per habit, so the new component reads `best` directly with no changes to the well-tested streak logic.
- **Page layout preserved.** Today section, `RadialCompletion`, and `HabitHistory` are untouched. New composition: Today вҶ’ (Radial 1/3 + Momentum 2/3 grid вҖ” radial on the left so the eye lands on the at-a-glance weekly % first) вҶ’ Streaks вҶ’ History. `allRegistryResult` query dropped (only the heatmap needed inactive habits for name lookup).
- **Loading skeleton rebuilt** in [web/src/app/(protected)/habits/loading.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/habits/loading.tsx) to mirror the new post-load shape вҖ” header, today check-in, 2-col momentum + radial, five hairline-separated streak row placeholders, so hydration doesn't shift.
- **README habits line updated** in [README.md](README.md) вҖ” "90-day heatmap, streak bar chart" вҶ’ "30-day momentum line, per-habit current + personal-best streak rows".
- **Responsive + tokens-only.** CSS-variable-driven throughout (no Tailwind color classes for theme colors); mobile 390px + both themes verified via Phase B universal system. No new dependencies; chart work reuses the existing primitives.

Propagates to every section label, weekly task/body-comp meta row, journal history preview, dashboard "yesterday" prefix, etc. вҖ” text reads cleanly on the watercolor canvas without reaching for text-shadow (retired in Phase A).

Replaces the blue "MB" stacked mark from before the amber palette. [(protected)/dashboard/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/dashboard/page.tsx) now passes `refreshStocks` + `refreshSports` into the masthead and no longer renders the footer. [dashboard-footer.tsx](web/src/components/dashboard/dashboard-footer.tsx) deleted вҖ” the duplicate bottom-of-page button is gone so there's one refresh affordance on the surface.
- **Body & Fitness latest-reading label is now time-aware** in [body-fitness-summary.tsx](web/src/components/dashboard/body-fitness-summary.tsx). Instead of hardcoding "today" (which was usually wrong вҖ” Oura/Fitbit data lags a day) or "yesterday" (wrong the moment a post-refresh sync pulls in today's real numbers), each cell now reads the actual date of its last non-null sample and renders `today` / `yesterday` / `Apr 15` accordingly. Cells degrade to `latest` when no date is available. Refactor also replaces the `todayValue` scalar with a `{ value, date }` pair from a new `lastNonNull` helper so weight, body fat, steps, and active calories each carry their own freshness label.
- **Mobile sticky `WindowSelector` blends with the watercolor canvas.** The `<div className="lg:hidden print:hidden">` strip in [dashboard/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/dashboard/page.tsx) dropped the solid `var(--color-bg)` fill for `background: transparent` + `backdrop-filter: blur(8px)`. Hairline bottom rule softened from `var(--rule)` to `var(--rule-soft)`.
- **Habits heatmap scaled up + contrast bumped** in [web/src/components/habits/heatmap.tsx](web/src/components/habits/heatmap.tsx). Cell size 14 вҶ’ 20px, gap 4 вҶ’ 5px so the 7-row heatmap lands at ~170px tall and visually balances the adjacent 140px radial panel. Missed cells lifted from `var(--rule)` to `var(--color-border)` so each square reads clearly against the watercolor bg. Legend swatches updated to match.
- **Tasks completion circle strengthened** in [task-item.tsx](web/src/components/tasks/task-item.tsx). 1.5px `var(--rule)` border вҶ’ 2px `var(--color-text-faint)` border on an 18px empty circle. Clearly visible on both themes against the watercolor bg.
- **Weekly Training table fits inside its 440px panel** in [(protected)/weekly/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/weekly/page.tsx). `Duration` вҶ’ `Dur`, `Calories` вҶ’ `Cal`; Date / Dur / Cal columns get explicit `width` (5.5rem / 3.5rem / 4.5rem) so Activity absorbs remaining width. `overflow-x-auto` wrappers removed (no longer needed); `whiteSpace: nowrap` replaced with `wordBreak: break-word` on the Activity column. Walk sub-table gets the same treatment.
- **Journal editor contrast lifted** in [globals.css](web/src/app/globals.css) + [journal-editor.tsx](web/src/components/journal/journal-editor.tsx). `.journal-field` rest-state `border-bottom` goes from transparent to `var(--rule-soft)` (focus deepens to `var(--rule)`), giving each textarea a visible boundary at rest. Placeholder color lifted from `var(--color-text-faint)` to `var(--color-text-muted)`. Prompt labels (Best moment / Biggest challenge / etc.) now render at `var(--color-text-muted)`; progress-row tabular count + Free-Write word count same lift.
- **Journal history entries clamp to 2 lines with inline Expand** in [journal-history.tsx](web/src/components/journal/journal-history.tsx). Preview text uses a `-webkit-line-clamp: 2` + `display: -webkit-box` clamp instead of Tailwind's `truncate` (which forced a single line and horizontal overflow). Long previews surface an inline "Expand" / "Show less" toggle that reveals the full preview without opening the structured body. Row restructured so the chevron+time toggle button and the preview+expand region are siblings вҖ” avoids nested interactive elements and keeps both click targets independent. The existing click-chevron-to-open-full-entry flow is preserved.
- **Tasks + Meals long text wraps (closes #305)** in [task-item.tsx](web/src/components/tasks/task-item.tsx) + [MealsClient.tsx](web/src/components/meals/MealsClient.tsx). `truncate` dropped from the task title and the `MealRowDisplay` dish-name span; both carry `wordBreak: break-word` + `minWidth: 0` so the full content is visible inline in the list. Row height grows naturally when text wraps.

### Changed (Impeccable UI revamp вҖ” Phase B В· Login, issue #294)

- **Hero header retokenized вҖ” first impression sets the bar.** The title is now a centered column: 40px `Logo`, then `<h1>Mr. Bridge</h1>` in `--font-display` (Hubot Sans) at `--t-h1` + weight 600 + `-0.02em` tracking, then the `Personal assistant` line in Mona Sans at `--t-meta` + `--color-text-muted`. Replaces the prior horizontal logo+title row at `text-2xl` with a hardcoded stack that never earned the two-column layout.

- **Form flattened вҖ” no card shell.** The form is a bare vertical stack with `var(--space-4)` gap; inputs are transparent + `1px solid var(--rule)` + `--r-1` + `.input-focus-ring` + `--t-body` type + 44px min-height, matching the Settings `FieldRow` treatment. - **Amber submit is the one accent on the screen.** Full-width `--accent` fill, `--color-text-on-cta` text, `1px solid --accent` border, `--r-1` radius, `--t-meta` + weight 500 + 0.02em tracking, 44px min-height, `var(--motion-fast)` + `var(--ease-out-quart)` opacity transition. - **Password show/hide enlarged to 44Г—44 touch target.** The eye toggle was 28Г—28 at `right-2` inside the input; now it's a 44Г—44 flat button pinned to the input's right edge with `hover-text-brighten` + motion-token color transition, and the input gains `paddingRight: 44` to clear it. `aria-label` + `aria-pressed` preserved.
- **OR divider hairline.** The demo alternate section leads with a `--rule-soft` hairline and a centered `OR` chip (`--t-micro`, 0.08em tracking, uppercase, `--color-text-faint`, `--color-bg` chip fill).
- **Demo button secondary.** Transparent background, `1px solid --rule`, `--color-text` label, 44px min-height, `--r-1` radius, `hover-border-strong` + motion-token transitions. Footer line (`Fictional persona В· read-write В· resets nightly`) stays `--t-micro` + `--color-text-faint`.
- **Auth-error banner retokenized.** The filled `--color-danger-subtle` + 1px border + `--r-2` card collapsed to a centered `--t-micro` `--color-danger` line bracketed by hairline `border-top` + `border-bottom` in `--color-danger` вҖ” quieter, reads as an inline notice rather than a card callout.
- **Tokenized through-and-through.** Every padding, gap, radius, font-size, and color references `--space-*`, `--r-1`, `--t-h1` / `--t-body` / `--t-meta` / `--t-micro`, `--rule` / `--rule-soft`, `--color-text` / `--color-text-muted` / `--color-text-faint`, `--accent`, `--color-text-on-cta`, `--color-danger`, `--color-bg`, and the motion / easing tokens. Zero inline pixel paddings beyond the 44px touch-target guarantees and zero hardcoded colors remain.
- **Touch targets verified вүҘ 44px** on every interactive surface: Email input (44), Password input (44), Show/Hide password toggle (44 Г— 44), Sign in button (44), Try the demo button (44).
- **No UX regressions.** Same `<Suspense>` boundary, same Supabase SSR auth, same safelisted `next` redirect param, same demo env gating, same email regex + password-trim validation gate and tooltip hint, same `auth_error` banner trigger, same show/hide password state with aria-pressed, same Enter-to-submit behavior.

Rest state is transparent with `--rule` border; saved state flips to a transparent / `--color-positive` treatment for the two-second confirmation flash. Button hover / disabled uses the shared motion tokens (`var(--motion-fast)` + `var(--ease-out-quart)`) instead of inline `transition-all duration-150`.
- **Hairline rows for list editors.** Stock-watchlist tickers and favorite-team rows are restructured as `<ul>` with `border-top: 1px solid var(--rule-soft)` between rows (none on first), 44px minimum row height, and a 44px Г— 44px `X` remove button at `--color-text-faint` with `hover-text-danger`. The outer `--color-border` card + individual row `border-bottom` hybrid is gone вҖ” rows now live inside the section's own rule rhythm. Search result rows carry a secondary 14px `--accent` `+` to preview what clicking will do.

Mode + protein sub-selectors rebuilt as the same compact inline pill group treatment used by the Appearance theme picker, shared via a small `<PillGroup>` helper colocated in the file. The `Apply` button matches the universal amber CTA vocabulary. Dismiss `X` target enlarged to 24Г—24 for reach.

Replaces the prior `24px` literal title and `14px` subtitle.
- **Section headers switched to `.db-section-label`.** The six `text-xs uppercase tracking-widest` / `--color-text-muted` / 0.07em paragraph labels (Profile, Fitness Goals, Nutrition Goals, Stock Watchlist, Favorite Teams, Appearance) now use the universal `.db-section-label` class вҖ” `--font-display`, `--t-micro`, weight 600, 0.14em tracking, `--color-text-faint`. The Nutrition Goals "Recalculate suggested macros" link sits in the section's right-side meta slot when the suggestion is dismissed.
- **Tokenized through-and-through.** Every padding, gap, radius, font-size, and color on the surface references `--space-*`, `--r-1`, `--t-h1` / `--t-body` / `--t-meta` / `--t-micro`, `--rule` / `--rule-soft`, `--color-text` / `--color-text-muted` / `--color-text-faint`, `--accent` / `--accent-soft`, `--color-text-on-cta`, `--color-positive`, `--color-primary` / `--color-primary-dim`, `--color-danger`, and the motion / easing tokens. Zero inline pixel paddings (beyond the 6px pin / 44px touch-target guarantees) and zero hardcoded colors remain.

### Changed (Impeccable UI revamp вҖ” Phase B В· Weekly, issue #291)
- **Weekly surface rebuilt against the universal vocabulary** across [web/src/app/(protected)/weekly/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/weekly/page.tsx) and [web/src/app/(protected)/weekly/loading.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/weekly/loading.tsx). Diff is JSX/CSS-only.
- **Card shells retired across the surface.** The six `rounded-xl` + `--color-surface` + `--color-border` + `card-lift` wrappers (Habits, Tasks, Workouts, Sleep & Recovery, Body Composition, Journal) plus the two inner `--color-surface-raised` callouts are replaced with flat `<section>` blocks that share the `db-section-label` header pattern and hairline `--rule-soft` separators. Copy generated from the same computed values already used for the tables below вҖ” no new queries or derivations.
- **Metrics recap rebuilt as hairline-ruled tables.** Each data category is a dedicated `<section>` with a `db-section-label` header that inlines its summary in `.meta` (e.g. "Habits В· 28/49 В· 57%", "Training В· 3 sessions В· 3h 20m В· 1,850 kcal", "Recovery В· 7 days В· readiness 78 В· sleep 82 В· HRV 41ms"). All tables use `borderCollapse: collapse`, 11px uppercase-tracked `--color-text-faint` headers, `--rule-soft` row hairlines, and tabular numerics via `tnum` on every numeric column.
- **Habits table** renders one row per habit: icon + name В· 7 day squares (14Г—14, `rx=3`, gap 4px вҖ” completed = `--color-text` at 0.85 opacity, missed = `--rule`, today = 1.5px `--accent` outline offset 2px, matching the Phase B heatmap vocabulary) В· `hits/7` tabular В· `streak` in `Nd` tabular.
- **Tasks section** splits into two hairline lists вҖ” "Closed this week" (up to 12, `вң“` glyph in `--color-positive` + truncated title in `--color-text-muted`) and "Still active" (up to 8, 6px `--accent` pip for overdue / `--rule` for on-schedule, trailing `fmtDate(due_date)` + "overdue" tag in `--accent` when past due). Both lists cap with a `+N more` tabular tail.
- **Training table** shows one row per structured session (Date В· Activity В· Duration В· Calories) with Calories right-aligned in `toLocaleString()` tabular. Walks render in a secondary sub-section below with `.meta`-styled header ("Walks В· N В· total time") and a reduced, `--color-text-faint` tabular table so they read as supporting context rather than peer sessions.
- **Recovery table** renders one row per day (Day name + date В· Readiness В· Sleep В· HRV) across `last7Days`, with today flagged in-row via a `--accent` uppercase "Today" pip and a weight-500 date. Missing cells render `вҖ”` in `--color-text-faint`. The three-tier positive/warning/danger scoreColor coloring is retired per the universal "one accent" rule вҖ” score values read as plain tabular figures.
- **Body composition table** shows Weight and Body fat as Metric В· Latest В· Prior В· О” columns. Delta cells use the `.delta-good` / `.delta-bad` / `.delta-flat` utilities (lower weight / lower body fat = good). Prior-measurement date trails below in `--t-micro` / `--color-text-faint`.
- **Journal section** keeps the qualitative consistency copy (Full week В· Strong consistency В· Halfway there В· Room to build В· Nothing logged) but drops the 52px big-number `--color-surface-raised` pill; the entry count and `missed` days now live inline in the `db-section-label`'s `.meta` span.
- **Loading skeleton retokenized.** [loading.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/weekly/loading.tsx) drops `SkeletonCard` / `SkeletonChart` for a reading-column placeholder (5 line shimmers at 62ch) followed by four hairline-table placeholders вҖ” mirrors the post-load layout so hydration doesn't shift.
- **Tokenized through-and-through.** Every padding, gap, radius, font-size, and color on the surface references `--space-*`, `--r-1`/`--r-2`, `--t-h1`/`--t-body`/`--t-meta`/`--t-micro`, `--rule`/`--rule-soft`, `--color-text`/`--color-text-muted`/`--color-text-faint`, `--color-positive`, and `--accent`. Zero inline pixel paddings or hardcoded colors remain.
- **No UX changes.** Same ten Supabase queries on the same tables in the same parallel batch, same 7-day rolling window ending today, same walk/workout partition, same readiness / sleep / HRV averages, same overdue-task flag, same body-comp delta vs the closest pre-weekStart measurement, same journal-count qualitative buckets.

### Changed (Impeccable UI revamp вҖ” Phase B В· Meals, issue #289)
- **Meals surface rebuilt against the universal vocabulary** across [web/src/app/(protected)/meals/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/meals/page.tsx), [web/src/components/meals/MealsClient.tsx](web/src/components/meals/MealsClient.tsx), and [web/src/app/(protected)/meals/FoodPhotoAnalyzer.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/meals/FoodPhotoAnalyzer.tsx). `/api/meals/log` (POST/PATCH), `/api/meals/analyze-photo`, `/api/meals/estimate-macros`, and `/api/meals/suggest` contracts are byte-identical; Supabase queries on `meal_log`, `recipes`, and `profile` preserved; tab navigation guard for unsaved scans, re-log prefill, recipe filter/sort, and the scanner log/meal-prep sheets are untouched. Diff is JSX/CSS-only.
- **Card shells retired across the surface.** The four `rounded-xl p-5` + `--color-surface` + `--color-border` wrappers around macro summary, logged-today list, quick-log form, and recent-meals list on the Today tab вҖ” plus the per-recipe card shells on the Recipes tab, the form + suggestion cards on the Plan tab, the per-date Past 6 Days cards, and the outer photo-analyzer frame вҖ” are all replaced with flat `<section>` blocks that use the `db-section-label` header pattern and `--rule-soft` hairline separators.
- **Meal log rendered as a flat hairline list with a tabular macros column.** Each meal row is a 44px-min row with the meal type chip (72px column, `--t-micro` / `--color-text-muted` / tabular), the food name (`--t-body`), a right-aligned tabular macro column (`{cal} cal В· P {x} В· C {y} В· F {z}`, `--t-micro` / `--color-text-faint`, min-width 220 on sm+ breakpoints), and a 32Г—32 re-log icon button. Rows separated by `border-top: 1px solid var(--rule-soft)`, no per-row card background. Inline edit mode reuses the same row slot with tokenized input borders.
- **Macro progress section rebuilt as hairline rows.** The four macro bars (Calories / Protein / Carbs / Fat) render as per-macro rows with a 3px progress track in `--rule-soft` and semantic fill (`--color-positive` вҶ’ `--color-warning` вҶ’ `--color-danger` as % climbs) вҖ” no card wrapper. Consumed / goal / remaining labels all use `tnum` for vertical numeric rhythm.
- **Recipes list flattened with a subtle on-hover lift.** Each recipe is a flat row with a `--rule-soft` top hairline between entries and the existing `.card-lift` utility applied for the 2px rise on hover. Card shells removed. Tag pills retokenized from `--color-primary-dim` filled pills to hairline `--rule-soft` chips that match the design system's "one accent" rule.
- **Photo analyzer frame dropped.** [FoodPhotoAnalyzer.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/meals/FoodPhotoAnalyzer.tsx) no longer renders inside a `rounded-xl p-5` + `--color-surface` + `--color-border` wrapper. The empty-state upload zone is now a `1px dashed var(--rule)` region with the Take Photo / From Library CTAs centered inside вҖ” a single dashed invitation rather than a filled card. Each scanned item is a flat row separated by `--rule-soft` hairlines. The combined-total readout renders as a hairline-topped/bottomed row with tabular numerics. Log / Meal prep sheets drop their inner `--color-bg` card fills and reveal as hairline-topped panels below the action row.
- **Inline spacing literals tokenized.** Every `padding: "Npx"`, `padding: "Npx Mpx"`, and `gap: N` literal in MealsClient (~20 sites) and FoodPhotoAnalyzer now references `--space-1`вҖҰ`--space-7`. Radii moved to `--r-1` / `--r-2`, font-sizes to `--t-body` / `--t-meta` / `--t-micro` / `--t-h1`, motion to `--motion-fast` / `--ease-out-quart`. Input borders switched from `--color-border` to `--rule`, backgrounds switched from `--color-bg` to transparent.
- **Page header retokenized** to the Phase B pattern вҖ” `.max-w-2xl` wrapper, `--font-display` + `--t-h1` + weight 600 title, `--t-micro` + `--color-text-muted` subtitle, `--space-5` margin below вҖ” matching Tasks, Habits, and Journal.
- **Tab bar preserved in pill form.** The four-way Today / Recipes / Scanner / Plan tab bar keeps the `--accent` active-pill treatment inside a hairline `--rule` wrapper; the Mode Toggle inside the scanner (Nutrition Label / Food Photo) uses the same pill vocabulary. Tabs re-tokenized to `--r-1` / `--r-2` / `--t-micro` instead of `rounded-lg` + `text-xs` literals.
- **Touch targets verified вүҘ 44px** on every interactive surface: tab buttons, meal rows (via `minHeight: 44`), re-log buttons (32Г—32 inside a 44-min row), Log / Estimate macros / Ingredients toggles, recipe expand buttons, Use-this-recipe + Log CTAs, scanner Take Photo / From Library / Camera / Enter manually buttons, Log sheet meal-type pills, and the Clear-all trash icon (32 inline inside a 44-min row).
- **No UX changes.** Same four tabs, same navigation-guard banner for unsaved scans, same re-log prefill from past meals, same recipe search + "use this recipe" log flow, same photo-scan вҶ’ add item вҶ’ log/meal-prep flow, same manual entry fallback, same "Ask Mr. Bridge" inline chat hand-off.

### Changed (Impeccable UI revamp вҖ” Phase B В· Journal, issue #286)
- **Journal surface rebuilt against the universal vocabulary** across [web/src/app/(protected)/journal/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/journal/page.tsx), [web/src/app/(protected)/journal/loading.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/journal/loading.tsx), [web/src/components/journal/journal-tabs.tsx](web/src/components/journal/journal-tabs.tsx), [web/src/components/journal/journal-editor.tsx](web/src/components/journal/journal-editor.tsx), and [web/src/components/journal/journal-history.tsx](web/src/components/journal/journal-history.tsx). - **Page laid out as a reading column.** The top-level wrapper switched from `max-w-2xl` to `.prose-column` (62ch cap) with `--space-7` rhythm between header, tab bar, and content. Page header retokenized to `--font-display` + `--t-h1` + weight 600 for the title and `--t-micro` + `tnum` for the date line.
- **Outer tab bar (Write / History) rebuilt as hairline underline.** The filled `--color-primary` pill group at the top of the surface is retired for a hairline `--rule-soft` bottom rule with a 2px `--accent` underline under the active tab. Tabs type as `--font-display` + uppercase + `0.12em` tracking + `--t-micro`, 44px min-height, `aria-selected` + `role="tab"` added for assistive tech. Inactive tabs sit in `--color-text-faint`; active tab rises to `--accent`.
- **Editor card shell dropped.** [journal-editor.tsx](web/src/components/journal/journal-editor.tsx) no longer renders in a `rounded-xl` + `--color-surface` + `--color-border` wrapper; content flows flat within the reading column. The `data-print-flat` attribute is preserved on the outer container so the existing `@media print` overrides still resolve correctly.
- **Inner tab bar (Reflect / Free Write) matches the outer treatment.** Same hairline underline vocabulary вҖ” amber 2px on active, `--font-display` uppercase micro label, 44px min-height вҖ” with the "SavingвҖҰ / Saved" indicator aligned to the tab-rule baseline on the right. Save-status copy switched to `tnum`/`--t-micro` and uses `--color-positive` for the saved moment, `--color-text-faint` otherwise.
- **Reflect prompts now render as document sections.** Each of the five prompts becomes a flat section: `db-section-label` header (uppercase micro-text), then a `.journal-field` textarea. Sections separated by a `--rule-soft` top hairline rather than card stacking. The five `--color-surface-raised` textareas with `--color-border` rings are retired.
- **`.journal-field` utility shipped** in [web/src/app/globals.css](web/src/app/globals.css). Fully transparent at rest (no border, no fill, no ring), with a single `--rule-soft` bottom rule that fades in on focus through a `--motion-fast` / `--ease-out-quart` transition. `outline: none` on both `:focus` and `:focus-visible` so the global 2px `:focus-visible` outline does not fight the quiet paper-ruling focus treatment вҖ” the color delta on the bottom rule provides the focus cue. Base typography: `--t-body` at 1.7 line-height.
- **Progress dots retokenized.** The five-dot row collapsed from 8px `--color-primary` / `--color-border` swatches to 6px `--accent` / `--rule` pips вҖ” same "filled = answered" semantic, quieter visual weight. Tabular `N / 5` count sits at `--t-micro` / `--color-text-faint` to the right.
- **Free-Write textarea retokenized** to the same `.journal-field` vocabulary at `--t-body` / 1.75 line-height with a right-aligned tabular word-count in `--t-micro` / `--color-text-faint` below.
- **Submit button** retokenized to `--accent` + `--color-text-on-cta` on `--r-2`, 44px min-height, full-width in the reading column. Motion references `--motion-fast` / `--ease-out-quart`; disabled-state opacity preserved at 0.5.
- **History rebuilt as a document-like accordion.** [journal-history.tsx](web/src/components/journal/journal-history.tsx) drops the per-entry `rounded-xl` + `--color-surface` + `--color-border` card stack for a flat list of `article` elements separated by `--rule-soft` hairlines. Each entry header is a 44px row with chevron В· `tnum` weekday + month + day timestamp (96px min-width column) В· truncated preview in `--color-text-faint`. Today's entry marks the timestamp in `--accent` + weight 600 (was filled background).
- **Expanded entries flow in the reading column.** Open bodies render inside `.prose-column` with a full-date `tnum` meta line, then per-prompt `db-section-label` / `--t-body` / 1.7 line-height prose blocks, and a final `Free write` section separated by a `--rule-soft` top hairline when present. `whitespace: pre-wrap` preserves the user's original line breaks.
- **Edit affordance preserved as a hairline row action.** The "Edit" button for past entries keeps the same click target (44px min-height) and the same server-action contract вҖ” only its fill / border chrome is dropped in favor of a `--color-text-faint` вҶ’ `--color-text` hover treatment. `aria-expanded` added to the accordion toggle; `<time dateTime>` wraps each entry date for machine-readability.
- **"Back to today" affordance retokenized.** When editing a past entry the top-of-editor breadcrumb row uses `--t-micro` + `--color-text-muted` for the link and `tnum`/`--color-text-faint` for the "Editing Mon, Apr 14" hint вҖ” 44px hit target on the back button, no behavior change.
- **Loading skeleton retokenized.** [loading.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/journal/loading.tsx) renders in the reading column with a hairline tab-bar placeholder and three hairline-separated prompt placeholders вҖ” mirrors the new post-load layout so hydration doesn't shift.
- **Print styles preserved.** The existing `[data-print-flat]` + blanket `textarea` print overrides in [web/src/app/globals.css](web/src/app/globals.css) continue to strip borders and fills and force 1.7 line-height for print. No changes to the print block; verified the `data-print-flat` attribute is still present on the editor wrapper.
- **Touch targets verified вүҘ 44px** on every interactive surface: outer Write / History tabs, inner Reflect / Free Write tabs, each history-row accordion toggle, per-entry Edit, Back-to-today, and the Submit CTA.
- **Tokenized through-and-through.** Every padding, gap, radius, font-size, and transition across the journal surface now references `--space-*`, `--r-2`, `--t-h1`/`--t-body`/`--t-meta`/`--t-micro`, `--motion-fast`, `--ease-out-quart`, `--rule-soft`, `--rule`, and `--accent`. Zero inline `padding: "Npx"` literals or `duration-NNN` classes remain under `components/journal/`.
- **No UX changes.** Same 5-prompt Reflect model, same Free Write surface, same 1.5s debounced autosave, same Submit вҶ’ clear вҶ’ switch-to-history flow, same past-entry edit-mode routing, same empty-state copy, same 31-entry history page. Draft saving, prompt logic, and the 7pm reminder are untouched.

### Changed (Impeccable UI revamp вҖ” Phase B В· Fitness, issue #290)
- **Fitness surface rebuilt against the universal vocabulary** across [web/src/app/(protected)/fitness/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/fitness/page.tsx) and the full [web/src/components/fitness/](web/src/components/fitness/) tree. Supabase queries on `fitness_log`, `workout_sessions`, `recovery_metrics`, `workout_plans`, `strength_sessions`, `strength_session_sets`, and `profile` preserved; the recovery query is broadened from `date,active_cal` to `*` over a 30-day floor so the new HRV/RHR/sleep panels render without adding new tables or columns. Inline set logger (`POST/DELETE /api/strength-sessions`), end-of-workout recap, weekly-plan expand/collapse, window-selector cookie flow, and workout-history sort/filter/paginate behavior preserved exactly.
- **Shared SVG chart primitives shipped** at [web/src/components/charts/primitives.tsx](web/src/components/charts/primitives.tsx): `ChartFrame`, `TrendLine`, `BarSeries`, `StackedBars`, `EndpointLabels`. One vocabulary: 1.5px primary stroke in `--chart-color-primary`, 1px dashed reference lines in `--chart-color-baseline`, 3px `--accent` today-dot with a 6px halo (18% alpha), stacked bars at 0.85 / 0.45 / 0.18 opacity on a single ink, today's bar wrapped in a 1px `--accent` hairline outline rather than recolored, implicit axes with only endpoint labels, and `font-variant-numeric: tabular-nums` on every numeric label. Charts measure their container via `ResizeObserver`.
- **Hover readouts on every chart.** Each primitive draws a hairline-bordered `--color-surface-raised` pill near the nearest data point showing "Apr 11 В· 166.4 lb" (line), the bar label + value (bars), or a two-line total + stage breakdown (stacked bars). Labels auto-flip below the anchor when too close to the top edge and clamp to the chart bounds on both sides. Native `<title>` hit-boxes remain for screen readers. Hovered bars also lift their fill opacity by 0.15.
- **Goal reference lines wired everywhere a goal exists.** `weight_goal_lbs`, `body_fat_goal_pct`, `weekly_workout_goal`, and `weekly_active_cal_goal` surface as dashed `--chart-color-baseline` reference lines on the Fitness page + the dashboard's Health Breakdown. Active-calories daily mode shows `goal/7` as a daily-target line; weekly mode shows the raw weekly goal. Sleep stages (7d) carries a dashed 8h target on both surfaces. Charts without an explicit profile goal (HRV, RHR, sleep efficiency) keep a trailing-average reference line.
- **Recharts removed from the Fitness page and Health Breakdown.** Every chart on both surfaces now renders from the new primitives. Recharts remains a runtime dep only for [web/src/components/dashboard/watchlist-widget.tsx](web/src/components/dashboard/watchlist-widget.tsx).
- **Body composition** ([body-comp-trends.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/body-comp-trends.tsx)) now ships Weight + Body fat as a two-column trend pair scoped to the top-level `WindowSelector` window. Goals from `profile.weight_goal_lbs` / `body_fat_goal_pct` render as dashed reference lines with inline "at goal / +N vs goal" readouts in each section header. (Muscle-mass trending is deferred until a sync source reliably populates `muscle_mass_lb`.)
- **Recovery panel** ([recovery-trends.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/recovery-trends.tsx)) ships the full health-breakdown vocabulary on the deep-dive page: HRV 30d (filled line with trailing average baseline), Resting HR 30d (line with average baseline), Sleep stages 7d (3-stack bars, Deep / Core / REM), Sleep total 14d (bars with 8h reference line), Sleep efficiency 14d (line from `metadata.sleep_efficiency`). Each chart tells you the latest value and its average inline in the header.
- **Activity section** ([activity-trends.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/activity-trends.tsx)) replaces the dual Recharts `BarChart` / `AreaChart` implementation. Daily mode renders workout-frequency bars (binary) + an active-calories line with a soft fill; weekly mode renders weekly-sum bars for both. Weekly goal renders as a dashed reference line; daily mode uses `goal/7` as the daily target line. The in-page granularity toggle now matches the `WindowSelector` vocabulary (accent background on the active pill, `--rule` hairline border, 32px min-height inline).
- **Weekly workout plan** ([weekly-workout-plan.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/weekly-workout-plan.tsx)) dropped its card shell. Each day is a flat row with a `--rule-soft` hairline separator and a 44px minimum click target on the expand toggle. Rest days render inline "Rest" in italic; today is marked with a 6px `--accent` pip + uppercase "Today" label (replaces the filled amber badge). Expand/collapse state, open-today default, exercise phase sections (Warm-up / Workout / Cool-down), set logger mount context, and end-of-workout recap remain unchanged.
- **Recent sessions** ([recent-sessions-list.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/recent-sessions-list.tsx)) restyled as a `db-row` list вҖ” 72-col date В· exercise-count / set-count / top-lift summary В· tabular RPE right-aligned. Card shell dropped.

- **Workout history table** ([workout-history-table.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/workout-history-table.tsx)) dropped its card shell. Filter pills re-tokenized to match the `WindowSelector` active-state pattern; table rows divided by `--rule-soft` hairlines; pagination buttons lifted to 44px minimum with tokenized borders. Sort/filter/paginate UX unchanged.
- **Health Breakdown on the dashboard** ([web/src/components/dashboard/health-breakdown.tsx](web/src/components/dashboard/health-breakdown.tsx)) now renders with the same primitives so the vocabulary between dashboard and `/fitness` is visually consistent. Readiness / Sleep / Activity score row retokenized with `--t-display` on Readiness and a shared scale on the others вҖ” amber appears only when readiness drops below 55. Recharts `ComposedChart` / `AreaChart` / `BarChart` stacks replaced by `TrendLine`, `BarSeries`, and `StackedBars`. Tab pills lifted to 32px min-height inside a `--rule` wrapper border. Metrics row (HRV / RHR / Total Sleep / Deep / REM / Steps) switched to tokenized typography; stress + resilience row preserved with hairline separators.
- **Dead files swept.** Deleted [web/src/components/fitness/body-comp-chart.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/body-comp-chart.tsx), [body-comp-dual-chart.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/body-comp-dual-chart.tsx), [body-fat-goal-chart.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/body-fat-goal-chart.tsx), [weight-goal-chart.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/weight-goal-chart.tsx), [active-cal-chart.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/active-cal-chart.tsx), [active-cal-goal-chart.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/active-cal-goal-chart.tsx), [workout-freq-chart.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/workout-freq-chart.tsx), [workout-list.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/workout-list.tsx), and [web/src/components/ui/granularity-toggle.tsx](web/src/components/ui/granularity-toggle.tsx) вҖ” all superseded by the new primitive-based charts and their inline granularity pills.
- **Touch targets verified вүҘ 44px** on the `WindowSelector` (already 44 from Phase A), granularity pills, weekly-plan expand buttons, workout-history filter pills (32 inline; OK inside a 44 row), prev/next pagination buttons, and every inline action.

### Changed (Impeccable UI revamp вҖ” Phase B В· Habits, issue #288)
- **Habits surface rebuilt against the universal vocabulary** across [web/src/app/(protected)/habits/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/habits/page.tsx), [web/src/components/habits/heatmap.tsx](web/src/components/habits/heatmap.tsx), [web/src/components/habits/streak-chart.tsx](web/src/components/habits/streak-chart.tsx), [web/src/components/habits/radial-completion.tsx](web/src/components/habits/radial-completion.tsx), [web/src/components/habits/habit-today-section.tsx](web/src/components/habits/habit-today-section.tsx), [web/src/components/habits/habit-toggle.tsx](web/src/components/habits/habit-toggle.tsx), and [web/src/components/habits/habit-history.tsx](web/src/components/habits/habit-history.tsx). All server actions (`toggleHabit`, `addHabit`, `archiveHabit`, `updateHabit`), Supabase writes on `habits` + `habit_registry`, optimistic update logic, streak computation, heatmap ratio logic, and the six parallel SSR queries are preserved exactly.
- **Card shells dropped across the surface.** Heatmap, streak chart, and radial chart no longer render in `--color-surface` + `--color-border` + `rounded-xl` wrappers. Each is now a flat `<section>` with a `db-section-label` header ("Completion Heatmap В· 90d", "Current Streaks В· N habits", "Weekly Completion В· 7d") and content separated from the next section by a `border-bottom: 1px solid var(--rule-soft)` on the page grid.
- **Heatmap rewritten with SVG primitives** ([heatmap.tsx](web/src/components/habits/heatmap.tsx)). 14Г—14px rounded squares (`rx=3`, gap 4px) matching the dashboard's `.habit-row .week` vocabulary. Missed days render `var(--rule)` at full opacity; completed days render `var(--color-text)` at 0.4 вҶ’ 0.85 opacity based on the existing 0вҖ“100% completion ratio. Today's cell gets a 1.5px `--accent` outline offset by 2px. Green-gradient scale (`--color-positive*`) retired. Hover-tooltip behavior preserved.
- **Streak chart replaced Recharts with hairline primitives** ([streak-chart.tsx](web/src/components/habits/streak-chart.tsx)). Each habit row now renders: name В· 1.5px `--chart-color-primary` horizontal stroke sized to `current / max(current)` В· 6px `--accent` dot marking the current endpoint В· dashed 1px `--chart-color-baseline` reference line at the non-zero average. Tabular current/best tallies right-aligned in `tnum`. Recharts `BarChart` + `ResponsiveContainer` import removed from this file; Recharts stays a dep for the fitness + health-breakdown charts that still use it.
- **Radial completion rebuilt as a single aggregate ring** ([radial-completion.tsx](web/src/components/habits/radial-completion.tsx)). 140Г—140px SVG, 4px stroke, `--accent` fill for the completed arc over `--rule` for the remainder, `stroke-linecap="round"`, 90В° start rotation. Centered `tnum` percentage in `--font-display` at `--t-h1` with a `N/M` day-count subscript in `--t-micro`. Below the ring, a hairline-ruled per-habit list shows `days/7` in tabular figures sorted descending. Recharts `RadialBarChart` + `Legend` import removed; three-tier `positive/warning/danger` rate coloring collapsed to a single accent per the universal "one accent" rule.
- **Today section retokenized** ([habit-today-section.tsx](web/src/components/habits/habit-today-section.tsx)). "Today В· N/M" header adopts the `db-section-label` + `.meta` pattern. Manage / + Add toggle buttons lifted from `py-0.5` (вүҲ16px) to `minHeight: 44px` + `--space-3` horizontal padding. Add-habit form drops its `--color-surface-raised` input fills for transparent inputs with `--rule` hairline borders and `input-focus-ring` for the `--accent` focus state; Save button now renders as a filled `--accent` CTA at 44px. Emoji-picker trigger sized to 44Г—44.
- **Habit toggle row rebuilt as a `db-row`** ([habit-toggle.tsx](web/src/components/habits/habit-toggle.tsx)). 44px row height with a 20px rounded-`--r-1` checkbox, lucide icon in `--color-text-faint`, optional emoji, name, and optional category label in `--t-micro`/`--color-text-faint`. Completion state fills the checkbox with `--accent` and strikes the name through in `--color-text-faint`. Edit / archive controls lifted to 44px. Hover uses `.hover-bg-subtle` (was a bespoke rounded-lg background).
- **History grid retokenized** ([habit-history.tsx](web/src/components/habits/habit-history.tsx)). 7d/30d cells now use a 14Г—14 rounded-square mark (matching the heatmap vocabulary) wrapped in a 44Г—44 transparent button for touch; today's cell gets a 1.5px `--accent` outline. 90d aggregated cells render `count` in `--color-bg` ink on a `--color-text` fill at opacity 0.4 вҶ’ 0.85 (replacing the green-gradient `--color-primary` variant). Row separation switched to `border-top: 1px solid var(--rule-soft)`. `aria-pressed` added for state exposure.
- **Page header re-tokenized.** Title uses `--font-display` + `--t-h1` + weight 600; subtext uses `--t-micro` + `--color-text-muted` with `tnum`. Sections separated by 48px vertical rhythm (`--space-7` gap in the chart grid) plus `--rule-soft` hairlines between section groups.
- **Touch targets verified вүҘ 44px** on every habit toggle row, Manage / + Add toggles, add-habit inputs + Save / Cancel, edit-mode inputs + Save / Cancel, archive вң•, WindowSelector (already 44 from Phase A), and every history cell button.
- **Tokenized through-and-through.** Every padding, gap, radius, font-size, and transition now references `--space-*`, `--r-1`, `--t-h1/body/meta/micro`, `--motion-fast`, `--ease-out-quart`, `--rule`, `--rule-soft`, and `--accent`. Tabular numeric columns flagged with `tnum`.
- **Dead file swept.** Deleted the unused [web/src/components/habits/habit-range-toggle.tsx](web/src/components/habits/habit-range-toggle.tsx) component вҖ” superseded by `WindowSelector` in Phase A and not imported anywhere else.
- **No UX changes.** Same check-off flow, same add/edit/archive flow, same streak computation, same heatmap data model, same 7/30/90/1y window-selector behavior, same optimistic updates. Diff is JSX/CSS-only.

A new `BodyFitnessSummary` renders a 4-cell 7-day-average grid (Weight, Body fat, Steps, Active cal) with hairline SVG sparklines вҖ” computed from the Supabase data the page already fetches, no new queries. ### Added (post-workout session logging вҖ” issue #249)
- **Two normalized Supabase tables** for actual workout performance: [supabase/migrations/20260416000000_add_strength_sessions.sql](supabase/migrations/20260416000000_add_strength_sessions.sql) creates `strength_sessions` (one row per session: user, plan link, performed_on, perceived_effort 1вҖ“10, notes) and `strength_session_sets` (one row per set: exercise_name, exercise_order, set_number, weight_kg, reps, rpe, notes). Weight stored in kg canonically; indexes on `(user_id, performed_on desc)` and `(session_id, exercise_order, set_number)`. RLS enabled on both вҖ” `strength_sessions` uses `auth.uid() = user_id`, `strength_session_sets` uses a join-through policy against the parent session. Tables named `strength_*` to avoid colliding with the existing `workout_sessions` table, which stores imported Fitbit/manual cardio rows.
- **`weight_unit` profile key** seeded at `"lb"` for every existing user ([supabase/migrations/20260416000001_profile_weight_unit.sql](supabase/migrations/20260416000001_profile_weight_unit.sql)); users can change it to `"kg"` via the existing profile upsert path. DB always stores kg; display respects the preference.
- **Inline set logging on the Fitness tab.** [web/src/components/fitness/inline-set-logger.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/inline-set-logger.tsx) adds weight/reps/RPE inputs under each today-only main-workout exercise in [web/src/components/fitness/weekly-workout-plan.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/weekly-workout-plan.tsx). Suggests the planned weight (converted from `weight_lbs` to the user's unit) as a pre-fill, auto-creates a session on first log, appends sets, and supports per-set delete.
- **End-of-workout recap.** [web/src/components/fitness/end-of-workout-recap.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/end-of-workout-recap.tsx) renders at the bottom of today's expanded card once a set has been logged вҖ” 1вҖ“10 perceived-effort selector + notes textarea, persisted via `PATCH /api/strength-sessions`.
- **Recent sessions section + top-3 sparklines.** [web/src/components/fitness/recent-sessions-list.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/recent-sessions-list.tsx) lists the last 10 sessions (date, exercise + set counts, top lift, RPE, truncated notes). [web/src/components/fitness/exercise-sparkline.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/exercise-sparkline.tsx) renders an 80Г—32 recharts line per top-volume exercise (sorted by cumulative `weight_kg Г— reps` over the last 90 days), with current top-set weight and delta vs. first session.
- **`/api/strength-sessions` route** ([web/src/app/api/strength-sessions/route.ts](web/src/app/api/strength-sessions/route.ts)) вҖ” POST appends a set (creating a session if today has none), PATCH writes the end-of-workout recap, DELETE removes a single set by `set_id`. Uses the SSR Supabase client so RLS enforces ownership automatically.
- **Unit helpers** in [web/src/lib/units.ts](web/src/lib/units.ts): `kgToDisplay`, `displayToKg`, `formatWeight`, `parseWeightUnit`. `WeightUnit` type threaded through the Fitness tab.
- **Fitness page wired end-to-end** ([web/src/app/(protected)/fitness/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/fitness/page.tsx)) вҖ” parallel-fetches strength sessions for the last 90 days, computes today's in-progress session + top 3 by volume, reads `weight_unit` from profile, and passes everything down.
- **New `StrengthSession` / `StrengthSessionSet` / `StrengthSessionWithSets` types** in [web/src/lib/types.ts](web/src/lib/types.ts).

### Changed (Bridge chat вҖ” issue #249)
- **New `get_workout_history` tool** ([web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts)) with optional `exercise_name` (case-insensitive partial) and `days` (default 30). Returns up to 30 recent sessions with per-set detail in kg. Registered in both the static system prompt and the demo prompt.
- **Progression heuristics added to the system prompt** (tool-only context вҖ” no history injected into every turn). Four rules v1: (1) +2.5 kg upper / +5 kg lower after 2 top-of-range sessions, (2) hold on RPE вүҘ 9 for 2+ sessions, (3) 10% deload on 2 missed-rep sessions, (4) suggest variation swap after 4+ flat sessions. Bridge is instructed to surface the evidence before recommending.

### Fixed (sports playoff / play-in schedule вҖ” issue #268)
- **ESPN schedule fetch now merges `seasontype` {2, 3, 5}** (regular + postseason + NBA play-in) in [web/src/lib/sync/sports/espn.ts](web/src/lib/sync/sports/espn.ts). Previously the fetch hardcoded `seasontype=2`, so once a team entered the playoffs the card would keep showing the final regular-season game (Warriors card stuck on a January game on 2026-04-16). New `fetchScheduleEvents` helper issues the three requests in parallel and dedupes by event id.
- **"Upcoming" filter tightened to reject past-dated events and `state === "post"` rows.** One Warriors regular-season game had `completed: false` but `state: "post"` (ESPN data quirk from a postponed/relocated event) and was leaking into the next-game slot. `espnGetUpcoming` now requires `!completed && state !== "post" && date >= now`; `espnGetRecent` symmetrically requires `(completed || state === "post") && date < now` so finished-but-not-completed quirks never appear as either "next" or "recent" when they belong to neither.

### Changed (persistent desktop chat sidebar вҖ” issue #267)
- **Chat session list is now always visible on desktop (вүҘ1024px).** Previously gated behind a History toggle in the page header, the sidebar in [web/src/components/chat/chat-page-client.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-page-client.tsx) is always rendered inside `hidden lg:block print:hidden` and sits as a sticky column next to the message thread. Sidebar and thread scroll independently вҖ” scrolling a long conversation no longer hides the "New chat" button or the history list. The old desktop History toggle button in the header is removed.
- **Collapse-to-rail chevron inside the sidebar.** [web/src/components/chat/session-sidebar.tsx](web/src/components/chat/session-sidebar.tsx) accepts `expanded` + `onToggleExpanded` props and branches its width between `280px` (expanded, full session list) and `56px` (rail вҖ” only chevron + New Chat Plus icon). Transition is a 180ms width ease. State persists to `localStorage` under the existing `chatHistoryOpen` key; default is expanded. Uses `PanelLeftClose` / `PanelLeftOpen` icons from lucide-react.
- **Mobile (<1024px) behavior unchanged** вҖ” `SessionSheet` drawer, hamburger, and FAB are untouched, so the mobile session-switcher reachability fix from #205 does not regress. Tablet 768вҖ“1023px stays on the mobile branch.
- `maxHeight` on the sidebar switched from the unused `var(--header-height)` subtraction to `calc(100dvh - 4rem)` matching the protected layout's actual 32px top + 32px bottom padding; `position: sticky; top: 2rem` anchors it during page scroll.

### Added (print styles вҖ” issue #264)
- **Global `@media print` block in [web/src/app/globals.css](web/src/app/globals.css).** Forces a light palette (white background, dark text, no shadows) by overriding all `:root[data-theme="*"]` tokens inside the print query вҖ” no matter which theme the user has selected, the printout is readable. Strips `<nav>` (desktop sidebar + mobile tab bar), resets sidebar margin on `<main>`, expands scrollable regions to full height, collapses `.grid` to single column, and applies `break-inside: avoid` to top-level widgets so cards don't split across pages. `@page { margin: 1.5cm }` sets the paper margin.
- **Chat bubbles flatten into a linear transcript in print.** `MessageBubble` wrapper carries `data-print-message-root=""` (left-aligned in print) and the inner bubble carries `data-print-message="user|assistant"`, which drives `::before { content: "You: " | "Mr. Bridge: " }` role prefixes. Bubbles lose their background, border, radius, and max-width so text reads as clean paragraphs.
- **Dashboard widgets reflow into briefing order when printed.** [web/src/app/(protected)/dashboard/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/dashboard/page.tsx) adds `print:flex print:flex-col` on the outer wrapper and `print:order-N` on each widget: Weather (1) вҶ’ Schedule (2) вҶ’ Tasks+Habits (3) вҶ’ Health (5) вҶ’ Today scores (6) вҶ’ Birthday (7) вҶ’ Watchlist+Sports (8) вҶ’ Emails (9).
- **`print:hidden` applied to interactive chrome** the global rule can't reach: demo banner ([nav.tsx](web/src/components/nav.tsx)), sync button + mobile window selector ([dashboard-header.tsx](web/src/components/dashboard/dashboard-header.tsx), [dashboard/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/dashboard/page.tsx)), watchlist/sports Refresh buttons, chat page header + history sidebar ([chat-page-client.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-page-client.tsx)), chat composer form + load-older + typing + error + tool-status bar ([chat-interface.tsx](web/src/components/chat/chat-interface.tsx), [tool-status-bar.tsx](web/src/components/chat/tool-status-bar.tsx)), mobile Sheet overlay/content ([ui/sheet.tsx](web/src/components/ui/sheet.tsx)), journal outer tab bar + "Back to today" row ([journal/journal-tabs.tsx](web/src/components/journal/journal-tabs.tsx)), journal editor inner tab bar + Submit button ([journal/journal-editor.tsx](web/src/components/journal/journal-editor.tsx)).
- **`data-print-flat` data-attr hook** on the journal editor card flattens its inline `border` / `background` / `border-radius` in print (inline styles win over Tailwind classes, so an attribute-selected `!important` rule is the clean escape hatch). Textareas lose their border/background and render as prose with 1.7 line-height.

### Fixed (mobile dashboard layout вҖ” issues #258 + #259)
- **Dashboard header stacks cleanly on mobile.** [web/src/components/dashboard/dashboard-header.tsx](web/src/components/dashboard/dashboard-header.tsx) now renders greeting + Sync button on line 1, date on line 2, weather on line 3 below the `lg:` (1024px) breakpoint; desktop row layout is preserved.
- **Time-range pills stick to the top on mobile.** [web/src/app/(protected)/dashboard/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/dashboard/page.tsx) renders a mobile-only sticky wrapper (`position: sticky; top: 0; background: var(--color-bg)`) containing the `WindowSelector` below the header, bleeding full-width via negative horizontal margins against the page's `px-5` padding. Desktop keeps the selector in the header's right column.
- **Sports card team rows stack vertically on mobile.** [web/src/components/dashboard/sports-card.tsx](web/src/components/dashboard/sports-card.tsx) `TeamRow` reshapes below `lg:` to logo (left-anchored) + three-line text stack (team name, next game, last result) + chevron (self-centered, right-anchored). Team names no longer truncate at 375px вҖ” `break-words` wraps; `lg:truncate` restores the desktop behaviour. Removed the inline `<style>` block that hid `.sports-card-league` at max-width 480px; the league subtitle is now gated via `hidden lg:block`.
- **`web/public/manifest.json` expanded** with 192/512 PNG icons, dark `theme_color` / `background_color` (`#0B0F19`), `start_url: /dashboard`, `display: standalone`, and `scope: /`.
- **App-shell service worker at [web/public/sw.js](web/public/sw.js).** Cache-first for `/_next/static/*`, `/icon*`, `/manifest.json`, and Google Fonts origins. Skips API, auth, and navigation requests вҖ” no data caching. Registered via [web/src/components/service-worker-register.tsx](web/src/components/service-worker-register.tsx), production-only (dev builds never register a SW).
- **`<meta name="theme-color">` wired via `viewport.themeColor`** in [web/src/app/layout.tsx](web/src/app/layout.tsx). Existing `metadata.manifest` and the auto-generated `<link rel="apple-touch-icon">` from `src/app/apple-icon.png` cover the remaining head tags.
- **[web/scripts/generate-pwa-icons.mjs](web/scripts/generate-pwa-icons.mjs)** regenerates `icon-192`, `icon-512`, and `apple-icon` from `src/app/icon.svg` via `sharp`. Run with `node scripts/generate-pwa-icons.mjs` when the SVG logo changes.
- Phase 2 (offline Supabase caching, queued writes, offline indicator) is out of scope вҖ” tracked for a future issue.

### Added (dark-mode OLED glow вҖ” issue #257)
- **Subtle text glow on headings in dark mode.** New `--text-glow` CSS token (`0 0 12px rgba(248,250,252,0.3)` in dark, `none` in light) applied to all `.font-heading` elements. Covers page titles, metric card values, score numbers, and nav labels. MASTER.md Key Effects updated to match.

### Fixed (UI/UX mop-up вҖ” issues #253 + #254)
- **Inline hover handlers replaced.** 5 remaining `onMouseOver/Out` sites in settings (profile-form, watchlist-settings, sports-settings) and dashboard (watchlist-widget) now use CSS utility classes (`hover-text-muted`, `hover-text-danger`, `hover-bg-subtle`, `hover-text-brighten`) instead of writing `.style.*` directly.
- **Hardcoded `color: "white"` tokenized.** 10 sites across chat, tasks, error pages, notifications, and layout now use `var(--color-text-on-cta)`.
- **`color-mix()` removed from MealsClient.** Replaced with existing subtle tokens (`--color-primary-dim`, `--color-positive-subtle`) for Safari <16.4 compatibility.
- **Mobile demo banner wrap-safety.** Added `overflow-hidden text-ellipsis whitespace-nowrap` to match the desktop variant.
- **Form focus/blur inline styles migrated.** New `.input-focus-ring` CSS utility in `globals.css` replaces `onFocus/onBlur` handlers in profile-form, watchlist-settings, and sports-settings.
- **CI token guards added.** `scripts/lint-tokens.sh` with 4 grep guards (onMouseOver/Out, hardcoded white, color-mix outside globals.css, raw hex outside allowlist) wired into GitHub Actions on PRs touching `web/src/`.

### Fixed (update_workout_exercise silent no-op on swaps вҖ” issue #239)
- **Bridge claimed it had swapped an exercise but the Fitness tab still showed the old name.** The `update_workout_exercise` tool's `updates` schema in [web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts) only accepted `sets | reps | weight_lbs | notes` вҖ” there was no way to change the exercise name. When asked to "replace Bent Over Row with DB Reverse Fly", the rename was dropped by JSON-schema validation, the UPDATE ran with an unchanged array, and Bridge confidently reported success. Schema now accepts `updates.exercise` for swaps/renames, and the tool returns an error when `updates` is empty so Bridge can tell the user truthfully instead of falsely confirming.

### Fixed (UTC date regressions вҖ” Fitness "TODAY" off-by-one)
- **Fitness weekly plan highlighted the wrong day after ~5pm PT.** [web/src/components/fitness/weekly-workout-plan.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/weekly-workout-plan.tsx) used `new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)` (UTC) to determine "today" and to build the MonвҖ“Sun week. After UTC rolled over, the "TODAY" badge jumped to tomorrow. Now routed through `todayString()` + `addDays()` from [web/src/lib/timezone.ts](web/src/lib/timezone.ts).
- **Repo-wide sweep for the same UTC slice pattern.** Replaced UTC-derived date strings in:
  - [web/src/components/fitness/active-cal-goal-chart.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/active-cal-goal-chart.tsx), [web/src/components/fitness/workout-freq-chart.tsx](web/src/components/fitness/workout-freq-chart.tsx) вҖ” daily/weekly bucket keys and labels.
  - [web/src/app/(protected)/fitness/page.tsx](web/src/app/(protected)/fitness/page.tsx) вҖ” MonвҖ“Sun week bounds for the workout-plans query.
  - [web/src/components/dashboard/trends-card.tsx](web/src/components/dashboard/trends-card.tsx) вҖ” window cutoff.
  - [web/src/lib/sync/stocks.ts](web/src/lib/sync/stocks.ts), [web/src/lib/sync/fitbit.ts](web/src/lib/sync/fitbit.ts), [web/src/lib/sync/oura.ts](web/src/lib/sync/oura.ts) вҖ” external-API date-range params (and Polygon bar timestamps via `Intl.DateTimeFormat` in `USER_TZ`).
  - [web/src/app/api/cron/reset-demo/route.ts](web/src/app/api/cron/reset-demo/route.ts) вҖ” demo seed dates and weekday detection.
  - [web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts) вҖ” demo calendar events and the `get_workout_plans` weekly tool query.
  - [web/src/app/api/google/calendar/route.ts](web/src/app/api/google/calendar/route.ts) вҖ” removed dead `today` constant.

### Fixed (chat agent loop вҖ” issue #223)
- **Bridge no longer ends a turn silently.** [web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts](web/src/app/api/chat/route.ts) `onFinish` previously skipped the DB write when the model produced no text (which happens when the AI SDK loop exhausts `maxSteps` on a tool step). It now synthesizes a deterministic summary from the executed `toolCalls` (e.g. *"Done. I updated a calendar event, created a calendar event."*) and persists that as the assistant turn, with a parenthetical note when the step or token cap was the cause. If no tools ran either, it persists a visible *"I hit a snag generating a response вҖ” please try again."* so the user is never left staring at silence.
- **Step cap raised 12 вҶ’ 20 with a token-budget guardrail.** Multi-step calendar/task flows were regularly hitting the old cap on the summary step. New `TOKEN_BUDGET = 150_000` tracked across steps via `onStepFinish`; when exceeded, an `AbortController` aborts the loop and the fallback-summary path takes over so cost stays bounded.
- **Diagnostic log on every turn completion.** `[chat] turn complete session=вҖҰ steps=N/20 tokens=вҖҰ durationMs=вҖҰ finishReason=вҖҰ hitStepCap=вҖҰ budgetExceeded=вҖҰ synthesized=вҖҰ` so we can see step-cap hits and fallback synthesis in production logs.

[web/src/components/settings/profile-form.tsx](web/src/components/settings/profile-form.tsx) aggregates dirty state across every `FieldRow` and invokes the hook. `FieldRow` now tracks a post-save baseline so dirty clears correctly once saved.
